1) < 1) attrs.push(`opacity=\"${g.opacity}\"`);\n    20→    if ((g.rotation ?? 0) !== 0) {\n    21→      const gb = bbox(g);\n    22→      const cx = gb.x + gb.w / 2;\n    23→      const cy = gb.y + gb.h / 2;\n    24→      attrs.push(`transform=\"rotate(${g.rotation}, ${cx}, ${cy})\"`);\n    25→    }\n    26→    const childSvg = g.children.map(c => renderElement(c, defs, embedImages, indent + \"  \")).join(\"\\n\");\n    27→    return `${indent}<g ${attrs.join(\" \")}>\\n${childSvg}\\n${indent}</g>`;\n    28→  }\n    29→\n    30→  // Leaf element rendering\n    31→  const hasFilter = el.type === \"image\" &&\n    32→    ((el.brightness ?? 100) !== 100 || (el.contrast ?? 100) !== 100 || (el.grayscale ?? 0) > 0);\n    33→  const hasShadow = el.type === \"image\" && ((el as any).shadowBlur > 0 || (el as any).shadowX || (el as any).shadowY);\n    34→\n    35→  // Build filter\n    36→  if (hasFilter || hasShadow) {\n    37→    const parts: string[] = [];\n    38→    let result = \"SourceGraphic\";\n    39→    if (hasShadow) {\n    40→      parts.push(`    <feDropShadow dx=\"${(el as any).shadowX || 0}\" dy=\"${(el as any).shadowY || 0}\" stdDeviation=\"${(el as any).shadowBlur || 0}\" flood-color=\"${(el as any).shadowColor || 'rgba(0,0,0,0.4)'}\" flood-opacity=\"1\" result=\"shadow\"/>`);\n    41→      result = \"shadow\";\n    42→    }\n    43→    if (hasFilter) {\n    44→      const sat = 1 - ((el as any).grayscale ?? 0) / 100;\n    45→      parts.push(`    <feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\" values=\"${sat}\" in=\"${result}\" result=\"gray\"/>`);\n    46→      const b = ((el as any).brightness ?? 100) / 100;\n    47→      const c = ((el as any).contrast ?? 100) / 100;\n    48→      const ic = (1 - c) * 0.5;\n    49→      parts.push(`    <feComponentTransfer in=\"gray\">`);\n    50→      parts.push(`      <feFuncR type=\"linear\" slope=\"${b * c}\" intercept=\"${ic}\"/>`);\n    51→      parts.push(`      <feFuncG type=\"linear\" slope=\"${b * c}\" intercept=\"${ic}\"/>`);\n    52→      parts.push(`      <feFuncB type=\"linear\" slope=\"${b * c}\" intercept=\"${ic}\"/>`);\n    53→      parts.push(`    </feComponentTransfer>`);\n    54→    }\n    55→    defs.push(`  <filter id=\"f_${el.id}\">\\n${parts.join(\"\\n\")}\\n  </filter>`);\n    56→  }\n    57→\n    58→  // Collect attributes\n    59→  const opacity = (el.opacity ?? 1) < 1 ? ` opacity=\"${el.opacity}\"` : \"\";\n    60→  const rotation = (el.rotation ?? 0) !== 0;\n    61→\n    62→  let cx = 0, cy = 0;\n    63→  if (rotation) {\n    64→    if (el.type === \"line\") {\n    65→      cx = (el.x1 + el.x2) / 2;\n    66→      cy = (el.y1 + el.y2) / 2;\n    67→    } else {\n    68→      cx = (el as any).x + ((el as any).width || 0) / 2;\n    69→      cy = (el as any).y + ((el as any).height || 0) / 2;\n    70→    }\n    71→  }\n    72→  const rotAttr = rotation ? ` transform=\"rotate(${el.rotation}, ${cx}, ${cy})\"` : \"\";\n    73→\n    74→  const filterAttr = (hasFilter || hasShadow) ? ` filter=\"url(#f_${el.id})\"` : \"\";\n    75→\n    76→  switch (el.type) {\n    77→    case \"rect\":\n    78→      return `${indent}<rect x=\"${el.x}\" y=\"${el.y}\" width=\"${el.width}\" height=\"${el.height}\" fill=\"${el.fill}\" stroke=\"${el.stroke}\" stroke-width=\"${el.strokeWidth}\" rx=\"${el.rx}\"${opacity}${rotAttr}/>`;\n    79→\n    80→    case \"line\":\n    81→      return `${indent}<line x1=\"${el.x1}\" y1=\"${el.y1}\" x2=\"${el.x2}\" y2=\"${el.y2}\" stroke=\"${el.stroke}\" stroke-width=\"${el.strokeWidth}\"${opacity}${rotAttr}/>`;\n    82→\n    83→    case \"image\": {\n    84→      let imgRef: string;\n    85→      if (embedImages && el.href) imgRef = el.href;\n    86→      else if (el.path) imgRef = el.path;\n    87→      else return \"\";\n    88→\n    89→      const bw = el.borderWidth || 0;\n    90→      const hasBorder = bw > 0;\n    91→      const fit = (el as any).objectFit || 'cover';\n    92→      const flipH = (el as any).flipH ? -1 : 1;\n    93→      const flipV = (el as any).flipV ? -1 : 1;\n    94→      const needFlip = flipH === -1 || flipV === -1;\n    95→      const fcx = el.x + el.width / 2, fcy = el.y + el.height / 2;\n    96→      const flipTransform = needFlip\n    97→        ? `translate(${fcx},${fcy}) scale(${flipH},${flipV}) translate(${-fcx},${-fcy})`\n    98→        : '';\n    99→\n   100→      let imgContent = '';\n   101→\n   102→      if (fit === 'cover' && (el as any).naturalWidth > 0 && (el as any).naturalHeight > 0) {\n   103→        // Cover: scale image to fill frame, crop via clipPath, position via cropX/cropY\n   104→        const frameW = el.width, frameH = el.height;\n   105→        const natW = (el as any).naturalWidth, natH = (el as any).naturalHeight;\n   106→        const zoom = (el as any).cropZoom || 1;\n   107→        const baseScale = Math.max(frameW / natW, frameH / natH);\n   108→        const scale = baseScale * zoom;\n   109→        const imgW = natW * scale, imgH = natH * scale;\n   110→        const cropX = (el as any).cropX ?? 0.5, cropY = (el as any).cropY ?? 0.5;\n   111→        const imgX = el.x - (imgW - frameW) * cropX;\n   112→        const imgY = el.y - (imgH - frameH) * cropY;\n   113→\n   114→        defs.push(`  <clipPath id=\"c_${el.id}\"><rect x=\"${el.x}\" y=\"${el.y}\" width=\"${frameW}\" height=\"${frameH}\"/></clipPath>`);\n   115→\n   116→        const gFlipAttr = flipTransform ? ` transform=\"${flipTransform}\"` : '';\n   117→        imgContent = `<g clip-path=\"url(#c_${el.id})\"${gFlipAttr}>\\n${indent}    <image x=\"${imgX}\" y=\"${imgY}\" width=\"${imgW}\" height=\"${imgH}\" href=\"${imgRef}\" preserveAspectRatio=\"none\"${filterAttr}/>\\n${indent}  </g>`;\n   118→\n   119→      } else if (fit === 'contain') {\n   120→        // Contain: fit inside frame, no clip\n   121→        const gFlipAttr = flipTransform ? 228→      // Reassign element IDs (recursive for groups)\n   229→      clone.nextId = reassignIds(clone.elements, 1);\n   230→      getDocuments().set(clone.name, clone);\n   231→   case \"to_front\":\n   530→          parent.push(el);\n   531→          break;\n   532→        case \"to_back\":\n   533→          parent.unshift(el);\n   534→          break;\n   535→        case 8;\n    42→  const fontFamily = args.fontFamily ?? \"Libre Baskerville\";\n    43→  const fontWeight = args.fontWeight ?? \"bold\";\n    44→  const fontStyle = args.fontStyle ?? \"normal\";\n    45→  const maxWidth = args.maxWidth ?? null;\n    46→  const lines = wrapText(args.text, maxWidth, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle);\n    47→  const tw = Math.max(\n    48→    ...lines.map((l) => measureTextWidth(l, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle)),\n    49→  );\n    50→  const th = fontSize * lines.length * 1.3;\n    51→  return { w: tw, h: th };\n    52→}\n    53→\n    54→/**\n    55→ * Resolve relative positioning params into concrete x/y values.\n    56→ * Returns resolved coordinates to merge into the element args.\n    57→ * Throws on errors (missing reference, no coordinates resolved).\n    58→ */\n    59→export function resolvePosition(\n    60→  doc: Document,\n    61→  type: string,\n    62→  args: any,\n    63→): ResolvedPos {\n    64→  const rel: RelativeArgs = {\n    65→    below: args.below,\n    66→    above: args.above,\n    67→    right_of: args.right_of,\n    68→    left_of: args.left_of,\n    69→    gap: args.gap ?? 0,\n    70→    center_h: args.center_h,\n    71→    center_v: args.center_v,\n    72→  };\n    73→\n    74→  const gap = rel.gap!;\n    75→  const canvas = doc.canvas;\n    76→  const result: ResolvedPos = {};\n    77→  const isLine = type === \"line\";\n    78→  const hasRelative = rel.below || rel.above || rel.right_of || rel.left_of;\n    79→\n    80→  // Get reference element bbox if relative positioning is used\n    81→  let refBox: BBox | undefined;\n    82→  let refEl: Element | undefined;\n    83→  const refName = rel.below || rel.above || rel.right_of || rel.left_of;\n    84→  if (refName) {\n    85→    refEl = findRef(doc, refName);\n    86→    if (!refEl) throw new Error(`Reference element not found: \"${refName}\"`);\n    87→    refBox = bbox(refEl);\n    88→  }\n    89→\n    90→  // ---- Vertical axis (below / above) ----\n    91→  if (rel.below && refBox) {\n    92→    const targetY = refBox.y + refBox.h + gap;\n    93→    if (isLine) {\n    94→      // offset y1/y2\n    95→      result.y1 = targetY + (args.y1 ?? 0);\n    96→      result.y2 = targetY + (args.y2 ?? 0);\n    97→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n    98→      // text y is baseline: add fontSize*0.85\n    99→      result.y = targetY + (args.fontSize ?? 8) * 0.85;\n   100→    } else {\n   101→      result.y = targetY;\n   102→    }\n   103→  }\n   104→\n   105→  if (rel.above && refBox) {\n   106→    if (isLine) {\n   107→      const lineH = Math.abs((args.y2 ?? 0) - (args.y1 ?? 0));\n   108→      const targetY = refBox.y - gap - lineH;\n   109→      result.y1 = targetY + (args.y1 ?? 0);\n   110→      result.y2 = targetY + (args.y2 ?? 0);\n   111→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   112→      // text: y is baseline, place so bottom of text aligns above ref\n   113→      result.y = refBox.y - gap;\n   114→    } else {\n   115→      // rect/image: place so bottom edge is at ref.y - gap\n   116→      const h = args.height ?? 0;\n   117→      result.y = refBox.y - gap - h;\n   118→    }\n   119→  }\n   120→\n   121→  // ---- Horizontal axis (right_of / left_of) ----\n   122→  if (rel.right_of && refBox) {\n   123→    const targetX = refBox.x + refBox.w + gap;\n   124→    if (isLine) {\n   125→      result.x1 = targetX + (args.x1 ?? 0);\n   126→      result.x2 = targetX + (args.x2 ?? 0);\n   127→    } else {\n   128→      result.x = targetX;\n   129→    }\n   130→  }\n   131→\n   132→  if (rel.left_of && refBox) {\n   133→    if (isLine) {\n   134→      const lineW = Math.abs((args.x2 ?? 0) - (args.x1 ?? 0));\n   135→      const targetX = refBox.x - gap - lineW;\n   136→      result.x1 = targetX + (args.x1 ?? 0);\n   137→      result.x2 = targetX + (args.x2 ?? 0);\n   138→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   139→      // text width depends on anchor\n   140→      const dims = textDims(args);\n   141→      const anchor = args.textAnchor ?? \"start\";\n   142→      if (anchor === \"end\") {\n   143→        result.x = refBox.x - gap;\n   144→      } else if (anchor === \"middle\") {\n   145→        result.x = refBox.x - gap - dims.w / 2;\n   146→      } else {\n   147→        result.x = refBox.x - gap - dims.w;\n   148→      }\n   149→    } else {\n   150→      const w = args.width ?? 0;\n   151→      result.x = refBox.x - gap - w;\n   152→    }\n   153→  }\n   154→\n   155→  // ---- Inherit orthogonal axis from reference ----\n   156→  if (refBox && refEl) {\n   157→    if ((rel.below || rel.above) && result.x == null && args.x == null && !rel.center_h && !isLine) {\n   158→      // Inherit x from reference element\n   159→      if (type === \"text\" && \"x\" in refEl) {\n   160→        result.x = (refEl as any).x;\n   161→      } else if (\"x\" in refEl) {\n   162→        result.x = (refEl as any).x;\n   163→      } else {\n   164→        result.x = refBox.x;\n   165→      }\n   166→    }\n   167→    if ((rel.right_of || rel.left_of) && result.y == null && args.y == null && !rel.center_v && !isLine) {\n   168→      // Inherit y from reference element\n   169→      if (\"y\" in refEl) {\n   170→        result.y = (refEl as any).y;\n   171→      } else {\n   172→        result.y = refBox.y;\n   173→      }\n   174→    }\n   175→    // For lines: inherit orthogonal axis as offset\n   176→    if (isLine && (rel.below || rel.above) && result.x1 == null && args.x1 == null) {\n   177→      if (\"x1\" in refEl) {\n   178→        result.x1 = (refEl as any).x1;\n   179→        result.x2 = (refEl as any).x2;\n   180→      } else {\n   181→        result.x1 = refBox.x;\n   182→        result.x2 = refBox.x + refBox.w;\n   183→      }\n   184→    }\n   185→    if (isLine && (rel.right_of || rel.left_of) && result.y1 == null && args.y1 == null) {\n   186→      if (\"y1\" in refEl) {\n   187→        result.y1 = (refEl as any).y1;\n   188→        result.y2 = (refEl as any).y2;\n   189→      } else {\n   190→        result.y1 = refBox.y;\n   191→        result.y2 = refBox.y + refBox.h;\n   192→      }\n   193→    }\n   194→  }\n   195→\n   196→  // ---- Canvas centering ----\n   197→  if (rel.center_h) {\n   198→    if (isLine) {\n   199→      const x1 = result.x1 ?? args.x1 ?? 0;\n   200→      const x2 = result.x2 ?? args.x2 ?? 0;\n   201→      const lineW = Math.abs(x2 - x1);\n   202→      const offset = (canvas.w - lineW) / 2 - Math.min(x1, x2);\n   203→      result.x1 = x1 + offset;\n   204→      result.x2 = x2 + offset;\n   205→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   206→      const anchor = args.textAnchor ?? \"start\";\n   207→      if (anchor === \"middle\") {\n   208→        result.x = canvas.w / 2;\n   209→      } else if (anchor === \"end\") {\n   210→        const dims = textDims(args);\n   211→        result.x = canvas.w / 2 + dims.w / 2;\n   212→      } else {\n   213→        const dims = textDims(args);\n   214→        result.x = (canvas.w - dims.w) / 2;\n   215→      }\n   216→    } else {\n   217→      const w = args.width ?? 0;\n   218→      result.x = (canvas.w - w) / 2;\n   219→    }\n   220→  }\n   221→\n   222→  if (rel.center_v) {\n   223→    if (isLine) {\n   224→      const y1 = result.y1 ?? args.y1 ?? 0;\n   225→      const y2 = result.y2 ?? args.y2 ?? 0;\n   226→      const lineH = Math.abs(y2 - y1);\n   227→      const offset = (canvas.h - lineH) / 2 - Math.min(y1, y2);\n   228→      result.y1 = y1 + offset;\n   229→      result.y2 = y2 + offset;\n   230→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   231→      const dims = textDims(args);\n   232→      result.y = (canvas.h - dims.h) / 2 + (args.fontSize ?? 8) * 0.85;\n   233→    } else {\n   234→      const h = args.height ?? 0;\n   235→      result.y = (canvas.h - h) / 2;\n   236→    }\n   237→  }\n   238→\n   239→  // ---- Explicit args always win ----\n   240→  // For non-line types, if x or y was explicitly provided and no relative override happened,\n   241→  // keep them. The caller should merge result over args, so we only set result if computed.\n   242→  // For lines: explicit x1/y1/x2/y2 are kept unless overridden above.\n   243→\n   244→  return result;\n   245→}\n   246→\n   247→/**\n   248→ * Check if relative positioning args are present\n   249→ */\n   250→export function hasRelativeArgs(args: any): boolean {\n   251→  return !!(args.below || args.above || args.right_of || args.left_of || args.center_h || args.center_v);\n   252→}\n   253→\n   254→// ---- Align ----\n   255→\n   256→type AlignAxis = \"left\" | \"center_h\" | \"right\" | \"top\" | \"center_v\" | \"bottom\";\n   257→\n   258→interface AlignArgs {\n   259→  ids: string[];\n   260→  axis: AlignAxis;\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→interface ElementDelta {\n   264→  id: string;\n   265→  props: Record<string, number>;\n   266→}\n   267→\n   268→export function computeAlign(doc: Document, args: AlignArgs): ElementDelta[] {\n   269→  const elements = args.ids.map((idOrName) => {\n   270→    const el = findRef(doc, idOrName);\n   271→    if (!el) throw new Error(`Element not found: \"${idOrName}\"`);\n   272→    return el;\n   273→  });\n   274→\n   275→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   276→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   277→\n   278→  switch (args.axis) {\n   279→    case \"left\": {\n   280→      const target = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x));\n   281→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   282→        const dx = target - box.x;\n   283→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   284→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   285→      }\n   286→      break;\n   287→    }\n   288→    case \"right\": {\n   289→      const target = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x + b.box.w));\n   290→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   291→        const dx = target - (box.x + box.w);\n   292→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   293→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   294→      }\n   295→      break;\n   296→    }\n   297→    case \"center_h\": {\n   298→      const minX = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x));\n   299→      const maxR = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x + b.box.w));\n   300→      const center = (minX + maxR) / 2;\n   301→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   302→        const elCenter = box.x + box.w / 2;\n   303→        const dx = center - elCenter;\n   304→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   305→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   306→      }\n   307→      break;\n   308→    }\n   309→    case \"top\": {\n   310→      const target = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y));\n   311→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   312→        const dy = target - box.y;\n   313→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   314→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   315→      }\n   316→      break;\n   317→    }\n   318→    case \"bottom\": {\n   319→      const target = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y + b.box.h));\n   320→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   321→        const dy = target - (box.y + box.h);\n   322→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   323→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   324→      }\n   325→      break;\n   326→    }\n   327→    case \"center_v\": {\n   328→      const minY = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y));\n   329→      const maxB = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y + b.box.h));\n   330→      const center = (minY + maxB) / 2;\n   331→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   332→        const elCenter = box.y + box.h / 2;\n   333→        const dy = center - elCenter;\n   334→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   335→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   336→      }\n   337→      break;\n   338→    }\n   339→  }\n   340→\n   341→  return deltas;\n   342→}\n   343→\n   344→// ---- Distribute ----\n   345→\n   346→interface DistributeArgs {\n   347→  ids: string[];\n   348→  axis?: \"x\" | \"y\";\n   349→  gap?: number;\n   350→  grid?: {\n   351→    cols: number;\n   352→    col_gap: number;\n   353→    row_gap: number;\n   354→    start_x?: number;\n   355→    start_y?: number;\n   356→  };\n   357→}\n   358→\n   359→export function computeDistribute(doc: Document, args: DistributeArgs): ElementDelta[] {\n   360→  const elements = args.ids.map((idOrName) => {\n   361→    const el = findRef(doc, idOrName);\n   362→    if (!el) throw new Error(`Element not found: \"${idOrName}\"`);\n   363→    return el;\n   364→  });\n   365→\n   366→  if (args.grid) {\n   367→    return distributeGrid(elements, args.grid);\n   368→  }\n   369→\n   370→  const axis = args.axis ?? \"y\";\n   371→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   372→\n   373→  // Sort by position on axis\n   374→  boxes.sort((a, b) =>\n   375→    axis === \"x\" ? a.box.x - b.box.x : a.box.y - b.box.y,\n   376→  );\n   377→\n   378→  const n = boxes.length;\n   379→  if (n < 2) return [];\n   380→\n   381→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   382→\n   383→  if (axis === \"x\") {\n   384→    const totalSize = boxes.reduce((s, b) => s + b.box.w, 0);\n   385→    let gap: number;\n   386→    let startX: number;\n   387→\n   388→    if (args.gap != null) {\n   389→      gap = args.gap;\n   390→      startX = boxes[0].box.x;\n   391→    } else {\n   392→      const extent = boxes[n - 1].box.x + boxes[n - 1].box.w - boxes[0].box.x;\n   393→      gap = (extent - totalSize) / (n - 1);\n   394→      startX = boxes[0].box.x;\n   395→    }\n   396→\n   397→    let currentX = startX;\n   398→    for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   399→      const dx = currentX - box.x;\n   400→      if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) {\n   401→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   402→      }\n   403→      currentX += box.w + gap;\n   404→    }\n   405→  } else {\n   406→    const totalSize = boxes.reduce((s, b) => s + b.box.h, 0);\n   407→    let gap: number;\n   408→    let startY: number;\n   409→\n   410→    if (args.gap != null) {\n   411→      gap = args.gap;\n   412→      startY = boxes[0].box.y;\n   413→    } else {\n   414→      const extent = boxes[n - 1].box.y + boxes[n - 1].box.h - boxes[0].box.y;\n   415→      gap = (extent - totalSize) / (n - 1);\n   416→      startY = boxes[0].box.y;\n   417→    }\n   418→\n   419→    let currentY = startY;\n   420→    for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   421→      const dy = currentY - box.y;\n   422→      if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   423→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   424→      }\n   425→      currentY += box.h + gap;\n   426→    }\n   427→  }\n   428→\n   429→  return deltas;\n   430→}\n   431→\n   432→function distributeGrid(\n   433→  elements: Element[],\n   434→  grid: { cols: number; col_gap: number; row_gap: number; start_x?: number; start_y?: number },\n   435→): ElementDelta[] {\n   436→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   437→  const startX = grid.start_x ?? boxes[0].box.x;\n   438→  const startY = grid.start_y ?? boxes[0].box.y;\n   439→\n   440→  // Compute max dimensions per column and row for uniform grid\n   441→  const cols = grid.cols;\n   442→  const maxColW = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.w));\n   443→  const maxRowH = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.h));\n   444→\n   445→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   446→\n   447→  for (let i = 0; i < boxes.length; i++) {\n   448→    const col = i % cols;\n   449→    const row = Math.floor(i / cols);\n   450→    const targetX = startX + col * (maxColW + grid.col_gap);\n   451→    const targetY = startY + row * (maxRowH + grid.row_gap);\n   452→\n   453→    const { el, box } = boxes[i];\n   454→    const dx = targetX - box.x;\n   455→    const dy = targetY - box.y;\n   456→\n   457→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01 || Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   458→      deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, dy));\n   459→    }\n   460→  }\n   461→\n   462→  return deltas;\n   463→}\n   464→\n   465→// ---- Shared: apply delta to raw coordinates ----\n   466→\n   467→function applyDelta(el: Element, dx: number, dy: number): ElementDelta {\n   468→  const props: Record<string, number> = {};\n   469→  if (el.type === \"line\") {\n   470→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) {\n   471→      props.x1 = r(el.x1 + dx);\n   472→      props.x2 = r(el.x2 + dx);\n   473→    }\n   474→    if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   475→      props.y1 = r(el.y1 + dy);\n   476→      props.y2 = r(el.y2 + dy);\n   477→    }\n   478→  } else {\n   479→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) props.x = r((el as any).x + dx);\n   480→    if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) props.y = r((el as any).y + dy);\n   481→  }\n   482→  return { id: el.id, props };\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→function r(v: number): number {\n   486→  return Math.round(v * 10) / 10;\n   487→}\n   488→"}]},"uuid":"a3a01901-14de-469d-b88b-24edcae6b764","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:20:31.263Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"c9d857c8-35a0-48f2-b300-c244d7fe46f9","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

{"parentUuid":"9d4fffea-fe0c-4fd4-8b99-f4dbe4acc1ca","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"61576487-1349-4f01-9df8-d7b4fbba612a","agentId":"a792f2c641a6b23ec","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01RCiCLAaj3r9gQQ1jKtqrsB","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→// ============================================================\n     2→// LAYOUT — check_layout: bbox, overlaps, bleed, spacing\n     3→// ============================================================\n     4→\n     5→import type { Document, Element, GroupElement, BBox } from \"./types.js\";\n     6→import { wrapText, measureTextWidth } from \"./fonts.js\";\n     7→import { flattenLeaves } from \"./tree.js\";\n     8→\n     9→export function bbox(el: Element): BBox {\n    10→  switch (el.type) {\n    11→    case \"rect\":\n    12→    case \"image\":\n    13→      return { x: el.x, y: el.y, w: el.width, h: el.height };\n    14→    case \"line\": {\n    15→      const x = Math.min(el.x1, el.x2), y = Math.min(el.y1, el.y2);\n    16→      return { x, y, w: Math.abs(el.x2 - el.x1) || 0.5, h: Math.abs(el.y2 - el.y1) || 0.5 };\n    17→    }\n    18→    case \"text\": {\n    19→      const lines = el.maxWidth\n    20→        ? wrapText(el.text, el.maxWidth, el.fontSize, el.fontFamily, el.fontWeight, el.fontStyle)\n    21→        : el.text.split(\"\\n\");\n    22→      const tw = el.maxWidth\n    23→        ? Math.max(...lines.map((l) => measureTextWidth(l, el.fontSize, el.fontFamily, el.fontWeight, el.fontStyle)))\n    24→        : Math.max(...lines.map((l) => l.length)) * el.fontSize * 0.55;\n    25→      const th = el.fontSize * lines.length * 1.3;\n    26→      let tx = el.x;\n    27→      if (el.textAnchor === \"middle\") tx -= tw / 2;\n    28→      else if (el.textAnchor === \"end\") tx -= tw;\n    29→      const ty = el.y - el.fontSize * 0.85;\n    30→      return { x: tx, y: ty, w: tw, h: th };\n    31→    }\n    32→    case \"group\": {\n    33→      const children = (el as GroupElement).children;\n    34→      if (!children.length) return { x: 0, y: 0, w: 0, h: 0 };\n    35→      let minX = Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;\n    36→      for (const child of children) {\n    37→        const cb = bbox(child);\n    38→        minX = Math.min(minX, cb.x);\n    39→        minY = Math.min(minY, cb.y);\n    40→        maxX = Math.max(maxX, cb.x + cb.w);\n    41→        maxY = Math.max(maxY, cb.y + cb.h);\n    42→      }\n    43→      return { x: minX, y: minY, w: maxX - minX, h: maxY - minY };\n    44→    }\n    45→    default:\n    46→      return { x: 0, y: 0, w: 0, h: 0 };\n    47→  }\n    48→}\n    49→\n    50→export interface ColorWarning {\n    51→  id: string;\n    52→  type: string;\n    53→  property: string;\n    54→  value: string;\n    55→  reason: string;\n    56→}\n    57→\n    58→export interface LayoutReport {\n    59→  structuralLayers: string[];\n    60→  overlaps: any[];\n    61→  outOfBounds: any[];\n    62→  bleedZone: any[];\n    63→  spacingGroups: any[];\n    64→  colorWarnings: ColorWarning[];\n    65→}\n    66→\n    67→export function checkLayout(\n    68→  d: Document,\n    69→  bleed: number,\n    70→  spaceTol: number,\n    71→  sizeTol: number,\n    72→): LayoutReport {\n    73→  const { w: cW, h: cH } = d.canvas;\n    74→\n    75→  const leaves = flattenLeaves(d.elements);\n    76→  const boxes = leaves.map((el) => ({ id: el.id, type: el.type, bbox: bbox(el), el }));\n    77→\n    78→  // Structural layer detection\n    79→  const canvasArea = cW * cH;\n    80→  const isStructural = (b: typeof boxes[0]) => {\n    81→    const area = b.bbox.w * b.bbox.h;\n    82→    if (area > canvasArea * 0.5) return true;\n    83→    if (b.type === \"rect\" && (b.el.opacity ?? 1) < 1 && (b.bbox.w >= cW * 0.95 || b.bbox.h >= cH * 0.95)) return true;\n    84→    return false;\n    85→  };\n    86→  const structuralIds = new Set(boxes.filter(isStructural).map((b) => b.id));\n    87→\n    88→  // 1. Pairwise overlaps (skip structural layers)\n    89→  const overlaps: any[] = [];\n    90→  for (let i = 0; i < boxes.length; i++) {\n    91→    for (let j = i + 1; j < boxes.length; j++) {\n    92→      if (structuralIds.has(boxes[i].id) || structuralIds.has(boxes[j].id)) continue;\n    93→      const a = boxes[i].bbox, b = boxes[j].bbox;\n    94→      const ix = Math.max(a.x, b.x);\n    95→      const iy = Math.max(a.y, b.y);\n    96→      const ix2 = Math.min(a.x + a.w, b.x + b.w);\n    97→      const iy2 = Math.min(a.y + a.h, b.y + b.h);\n    98→      if (ix < ix2 && iy < iy2) {\n    99→        const iw = Math.round((ix2 - ix) * 10) / 10;\n   100→        const ih = Math.round((iy2 - iy) * 10) / 10;\n   101→        overlaps.push({\n   102→          a: boxes[i].id,\n   103→          b: boxes[j].id,\n   104→          a_type: boxes[i].type,\n   105→          b_type: boxes[j].type,\n   106→          intersection: { x: Math.round(ix * 10) / 10, y: Math.round(iy * 10) / 10, w: iw, h: ih },\n   107→          area_mm2: Math.round(iw * ih * 10) / 10,\n   108→        });\n   109→      }\n   110→    }\n   111→  }\n   112→\n   113→  // 2. Out of bounds\n   114→  const outOfBounds: any[] = [];\n   115→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   116→    const { x, y, w, h } = b.bbox;\n   117→    const sides: any[] = [];\n   118→    if (x < 0) sides.push({ side: \"left\", overflow_mm: Math.round(-x * 10) / 10 });\n   119→    if (y < 0) sides.push({ side: \"top\", overflow_mm: Math.round(-y * 10) / 10 });\n   120→    if (x + w > cW) sides.push({ side: \"right\", overflow_mm: Math.round((x + w - cW) * 10) / 10 });\n   121→    if (y + h > cH) sides.push({ side: \"bottom\", overflow_mm: Math.round((y + h - cH) * 10) / 10 });\n   122→    for (const s of sides) outOfBounds.push({ id: b.id, ...s });\n   123→  }\n   124→\n   125→  // 3. Bleed zone\n   126→  const bleedZone: any[] = [];\n   127→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   128→    const { x, y, w, h } = b.bbox;\n   129→    if (w >= cW * 0.95 && h >= cH * 0.95) continue;\n   130→    const sides: any[] = [];\n   131→    if (x > 0 && x < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"left\", distance_mm: Math.round(x * 10) / 10 });\n   132→    if (y > 0 && y < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"top\", distance_mm: Math.round(y * 10) / 10 });\n   133→    if (x + w < cW && cW - (x + w) < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"right\", distance_mm: Math.round((cW - x - w) * 10) / 10 });\n   134→    if (y + h < cH && cH - (y + h) < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"bottom\", distance_mm: Math.round((cH - y - h) * 10) / 10 });\n   135→    for (const s of sides) bleedZone.push({ id: b.id, ...s });\n   136→  }\n   137→\n   138→  // 4. Spacing groups\n   139→  const spacingGroups: any[] = [];\n   140→  const sizeKey = (b: typeof boxes[0]) => `${b.type}_${Math.round(b.bbox.w / sizeTol) * sizeTol}_${Math.round(b.bbox.h / sizeTol) * sizeTol}`;\n   141→  const groups = new Map<string, typeof boxes>();\n   142→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   143→    const k = sizeKey(b);\n   144→    if (!groups.has(k)) groups.set(k, []);\n   145→    groups.get(k)!.push(b);\n   146→  }\n   147→  for (const [, members] of groups) {\n   148→    if (members.length < 3) continue;\n   149→    const ys = members.map((m) => m.bbox.y);\n   150→    const ySpread = Math.max(...ys) - Math.min(...ys);\n   151→    const xs = members.map((m) => m.bbox.x);\n   152→    const xSpread = Math.max(...xs) - Math.min(...xs);\n   153→\n   154→    if (xSpread > ySpread) {\n   155→      const sorted = [...members].sort((a, b) => a.bbox.x - b.bbox.x);\n   156→      const gaps: number[] = [];\n   157→      for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {\n   158→        gaps.push(Math.round((sorted[i].bbox.x - sorted[i - 1].bbox.x - sorted[i - 1].bbox.w) * 10) / 10);\n   159→      }\n   160→      const avgGap = gaps.reduce((s, g) => s + g, 0) / gaps.length;\n   161→      const uniform = gaps.every((g) => Math.abs(g - avgGap) <= spaceTol);\n   162→      spacingGroups.push({\n   163→        ids: sorted.map((m) => m.id),\n   164→        type: members[0].type,\n   165→        axis: \"horizontal\",\n   166→        gaps_mm: gaps,\n   167→        avg_gap_mm: Math.round(avgGap * 10) / 10,\n   168→        uniform,\n   169→      });\n   170→    } else {\n   171→      const sorted = [...members].sort((a, b) => a.bbox.y - b.bbox.y);\n   172→      const gaps: number[] = [];\n   173→      for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {\n   174→        gaps.push(Math.round((sorted[i].bbox.y - sorted[i - 1].bbox.y - sorted[i - 1].bbox.h) * 10) / 10);\n   175→      }\n   176→      const avgGap = gaps.reduce((s, g) => s + g, 0) / gaps.length;\n   177→      const uniform = gaps.every((g) => Math.abs(g - avgGap) <= spaceTol);\n   178→      spacingGroups.push({\n   179→        ids: sorted.map((m) => m.id),\n   180→        type: members[0].type,\n   181→        axis: \"vertical\",\n   182→        gaps_mm: gaps,\n   183→        avg_gap_mm: Math.round(avgGap * 10) / 10,\n   184→        uniform,\n   185→      });\n   186→    }\n   187→  }\n   188→\n   189→  // 5. CMYK color warnings\n   190→  const colorWarnings: ColorWarning[] = [];\n   191→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   192→    const el = b.el;\n   193→    const colorProps: [string, string | undefined][] = [\n   194→      [\"fill\", (el as any).fill],\n   195→      [\"stroke\", (el as any).stroke],\n   196→      [\"borderColor\", (el as any).borderColor],\n   197→      [\"shadowColor\", (el as any).shadowColor],\n   198→    ];\n   199→    for (const [prop, val] of colorProps) {\n   200→      if (!val || val === \"none\") continue;\n   201→      if (/^rgba?\\s*\\(/.test(val) && /,\\s*[\\d.]+\\s*\\)$/.test(val) && !/,\\s*1\\s*\\)$/.test(val)) {\n   202→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Transparence (alpha) non supportée en CMJN\" });\n   203→      }\n   204→      if (/^hsla?\\s*\\(/.test(val)) {\n   205→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Couleur HSL — convertir en hex pour l'impression\" });\n   206→      }\n   207→      if (val === \"#000000\" || val === \"#000\" || val.toLowerCase() === \"black\") {\n   208→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Noir pur — utiliser un noir riche (ex: #1C1C1C) pour l'impression\" });\n   209→      }\n   210→      // Detect highly saturated colors likely out of CMYK gamut\n   211→      const hex = parseHex(val);\n   212→      if (hex) {\n   213→        const [r, g, _b] = hex;\n   214→        const max = Math.max(r, g, _b);\n   215→        const min = Math.min(r, g, _b);\n   216→        if (max === 255 && min === 0 && (r === 0 || g === 0 || _b === 0)) {\n   217→          colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Couleur très saturée — hors gamut CMJN probable\" });\n   218→        }\n   219→      }\n   220→    }\n   221→  }\n   222→\n   223→  return { structuralLayers: [...structuralIds], overlaps, outOfBounds, bleedZone, spacingGroups, colorWarnings };\n   224→}\n   225→\n   226→function parseHex(val: string): [number, number, number] | null {\n   227→  const m3 = val.match(/^#([0-9a-f])([0-9a-f])([0-9a-f])$/i);\n   228→  if (m3) return [parseInt(m3[1] + m3[1], 16), parseInt(m3[2] + m3[2], 16), parseInt(m3[3] + m3[3], 16)];\n   229→  const m6 = val.match(/^#([0-9a-f]{2})([0-9a-f]{2})([0-9a-f]{2})$/i);\n   230→  if (m6) return [parseInt(m6[1], 16), parseInt(m6[2], 16), parseInt(m6[3], 16)];\n   231→  return null;\n   232→}\n (selLine) lines.push(selLine);\n    92→  lines.push(\"─\".repeat(60));\n    93→\n    94→  function renderEl(el: Element, indent: number): void {\n    95→    const pad = \"  \".repeat(indent);\n    96→    const nameTag = el.name ? ` (${el.name})` : \"\";\n    97→    const id = el.id + nameTag;\n    98→    let info: string;\n    99→\n   100→    switch (el.type) {\n   101→      case \"group\": {\n   102→        const g = el as GroupElement;\n   103→        info = `group  [${g.children.length} children]`;\n   104→        if (el.opacity < 1) info += ` op:${el.opacity}`;\n   105→        if (el.rotation) info += ` rot:${el.rotation}`;\n   106→        lines.push(`${pad}${id.padEnd(Math.max(1, 20 - indent * 2))} ${info}`);\n   107→        for (const child of g.children) renderEl(child, indent + 1);\n   108→        return;\n   109→      }\n   110→      case \"text\": {\n   111→        const preview = el.text.length > 25 ? el.text.slice(0, 24) + \"…\" : el.text;\n   112→        const props = [`sz:${el.fontSize}`, el.textAnchor !== \"start\" ? el.textAnchor.slice(0, 3) : \"\", `fill:${el.fill}`];\n   113→        if (el.maxWidth) props.push(`mw:${el.maxWidth}`);\n   114→        info = `text   \"${preview}\"  x:${r(el.x)} y:${r(el.y)}  ${props.filter(Boolean).join(\" \")}`;\n   115→        break;\n   116→      }\n   117→      case \"image\": {\n   118→        const fname = el.path || \"?\";\n   119→        info = `image  ${fname}  x:${r(el.x)} y:${r(el.y)}  ${r(el.width)}×${r(el.height)}`;\n   120→        if (el.opacity < 1) info += ` op:${el.opacity}`;\n   121→        break;\n   122→      }\n   123→      case \"rect\":\n   124→        info = `rect   x:${r(el.x)} y:${r(el.y)}  ${r(el.width)}×${r(el.height)}  fill:${el.fill}`;\n   125→        if (el.stroke !== \"none\") info += ` stroke:${el.stroke}`;\n   126→        break;\n   127→      case \"line\":\n   128→        info = `line   ${r(el.x1)},${r(el.y1)}→${r(el.x2)},${r(el.y2)}  stroke:${el.stroke} w:${el.strokeWidth}`;\n   129→        break;\n   130→      default:\n   131→        info = `${el.type}`;\n   132→    }\n   133→\n   134→    if (el.opacity < 1 && el.type !== \"image\") info += ` op:${el.opacity}`;\n   135→    if (el.rotation) info += ` rot:${el.rotation}`;\n   136→\n   137→    lines.push(`${pad}${id.padEnd(Math.max(1, 20 - indent * 2))} ${info}`);\n   138→  }\n   139→\n   140→  for (const el of d.elements) renderEl(el, 0);\n   141→\n   142→  return lines.join(\"\\n\");\n   143→}\n   144→\n   145→function r(v: number): number { return Math.round(v * 10) / 10; }\n   146→\n   147→export async function handleTool(name: string, args: any) {\n   148→  switch (name) {\n   149→    // ---- Documents ----\n   150→    case \"doc_new\": {\n   151→      const fmt = args.format || \"A3\";\n   152→      const f = FORMATS[fmt] || FORMATS.A3;\n   153→      const orient = args.orientation || \"portrait\";\n   154→      const isL = orient === \"paysage\" && !SCREEN_FORMATS.has(fmt);\n   155→      const w = isL ? f.h : f.w, h = isL ? f.w : f.h;\n   156→      const newDoc = {\n   157→        name: args.name,\n   158→        category: args.category || \"general\",\n   159→        canvas: { format: fmt, orientation: orient, w, h, bg: args.background || \"#ffffff\" },\n   160→        meta: {},\n   161→        elements: [] as any[],\n   162→        nextId: 1,\n   163→      };\n   164→      getDocuments().set(args.name, newDoc);\n   165→      setActiveDoc(args.name);\n   166→      bus.emit(\"document:created\", { name: args.name });\n   167→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `Nouveau document \"${args.name}\" (${fmt} ${orient})`, level: \"success\" });\n   168→      return txt(`New doc \"${args.name}\" [${newDoc.category}] (${fmt} ${orient} ${w}x${h}mm)`);\n   169→    }\n   170→\n   171→    case \"doc_save\": {\n   172→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   173→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   174→      if (args.name && args.name !== d.name) {\n   175→        d.name = args.name;\n   176→        getDocuments().delete(getActiveDocName()!);\n   177→        getDocuments().set(args.name, d);\n   178→        setActiveDoc(args.name);\n   179→      }\n   180→      saveDocToDisk(d);\n   181→      bus.emit(\"document:saved\", { name: d.name });\n   182→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `Document \"${d.name}\" sauvegardé`, level: \"success\" });\n   183→      return txt(`Saved \"${d.name}\" → DB`);\n   184→    }\n   185→\n   186→    case \"doc_load\": {\n   187→      const documents = getDocuments();\n   188→      if (!documents.has(args.name)) {\n   189→        const doc = getStore().loadOne(args.name);\n   190→        if (!doc) return txt(`Document \"${args.name}\" not found`);\n   191→        documents.set(doc.name, doc);\n   192→      }\n   193→      setActiveDoc(args.name);\n   194→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   195→      bus.emit(\"document:loaded\", { name: args.name });\n   196→      return txt(`Loaded \"${d!.name}\" (${d!.canvas.format}, ${countElements(d!.elements)} elements)`);\n   197→    }\n   198→\n   199→    case \"doc_list\": {\n   200→      const list = getDocList();\n   201→      if (!list.length) return txt(\"No documents.\");\n   202→      const lines = list.map(\n   203→        (d) => `- ${d.name} [${d.category}] (${d.format}, ${d.count} elements)`\n   204→      );\n   205→      return txt(lines.join(\"\\n\"));\n   206→    }\n   207→\n   208→    case \"doc_delete\": {\n   209→      const documents = getDocuments();\n   210→      if (!documents.has(args.name)) return txt(`Document \"${args.name}\" not found`);\n   211→      if (documents.size <= 1) return txt(`Cannot delete the only document`);\n   212→      const wasActive = getActiveDocName() === args.name;\n   213→      deleteDocument(args.name);\n   214→      bus.emit(\"document:deleted\", { name: args.name });\n   215→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `Document \"${args.name}\" supprimé`, level: \"info\" });\n   216→      if (wasActive) bus.emit(\"document:loaded\", { name: getActiveDocName() });\n   217→      return txt(`Deleted \"${args.name}\"${wasActive ? ` → switched to \"${getActiveDocName()}\"` : \"\"}`);\n   218→    }\n   219→\n   220→    case \"doc_duplicate\": {\n   221→      const sourceName = args.source || getActiveDocName();\n   222→      if (!sourceName) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   223→      const sourceDoc = getDocuments().get(sourceName);\n   224→      if (!sourceDoc) return txt(`Document \"${sourceName}\" not found`);\n   225→      if (getDocuments().has(args.name)) return txt(`Document \"${args.name}\" already exists`);\n   226→      const clone = structuredClone(sourceDoc);\n   227→      clone.name = args.name;\n   228→      // Reassign element IDs (recursive for groups)\n   229→      clone.nextId = reassignIds(clone.elements, 1);\n   230→      getDocuments().set(clone.name, clone);\n   231→      setActiveDoc(clone.name);\n   232→      saveDocToDisk(clone);\n   233→      bus.emit(\"document:created\", { name: clone.name });\n   234→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `Document \"${sourceName}\" cloné → \"${clone.name}\"`, level: \"success\" });\n   235→      return txt(`Cloned \"${sourceName}\" → \"${clone.name}\" (${clone.elements.length} elements)`);\n   236→    }\n   237→\n   238→    case \"doc_rename\": {\n   239→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   240→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   241→      if (getDocuments().has(args.name)) return txt(`Document \"${args.name}\" already exists`);\n   242→      const oldName = d.name;\n   243→      getStore().deleteDoc(oldName);\n   244→      getDocuments().delete(oldName);\n   245→      d.name = args.name;\n   246→      getDocuments().set(args.name, d);\n   247→      setActiveDoc(args.name);\n   248→      saveDocToDisk(d);\n   249→      bus.emit(\"document:loaded\", { name: args.name });\n   250→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `\"${oldName}\" → \"${args.name}\"`, level: \"success\" });\n   251→      return txt(`Renamed \"${oldName}\" → \"${args.name}\"`);\n   252→    }\n   253→\n   254→    case \"element_duplicate\": {\n   255→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   256→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   257→      const el = findEl(d, args.id_or_name);\n   258→      if (!el) return txt(`Element \"${args.id_or_name}\" not found`);\n   259→      const clone = structuredClone(el);\n   260→      // Reassign IDs recursively for groups\n   261→      if (clone.type === \"group\") {\n   262→        clone.id = `e${d.nextId++}`;\n   263→        d.nextId = reassignIds((clone as GroupElement).children, d.nextId);\n   264→      } else {\n   265→        clone.id = `e${d.nextId++}`;\n   266→      }\n   267→      delete clone.name;\n   268→      delete (clone as any).href;\n   269→      const dx = args.offset_x ?? 5;\n   270→      const dy = args.offset_y ?? 5;\n   271→      applyOffset(clone, dx, dy);\n   272→      d.elements.push(clone);\n   273→      markDirty();\n   274→      bus.emit(\"element:added\", { id: clone.id });\n   275→      return txt(`Duplicated \"${args.id_or_name}\" → ${clone.id} (offset +${dx},+${dy}mm)`);\n   276→    }\n   277→\n   278→    // ---- Assets ----\n   279→    case \"list_assets\": {\n   280→      const files = listAssets();\n   281→      if (!files.length) return txt(`No images in ${relative(PROJECT_ROOT, ASSETS_DIR)}/`);\n   282→      return txt(`Assets (${ASSETS_DIR}):\\n${files.map((f) => `- ${f}`).join(\"\\n\")}`);\n   283→    }\n   284→\n   285→    // ---- Canvas ----\n   286→    case \"canvas_setup\": {\n   287→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   288→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   289→      const fmt = args.format || d.canvas.format;\n   290→      const f = FORMATS[fmt] || FORMATS.A3;\n   291→      const orient = args.orientation || d.canvas.orientation || \"portrait\";\n   292→      const isL = orient === \"paysage\" && !SCREEN_FORMATS.has(fmt);\n   293→      const w = isL ? f.h : f.w, h = isL ? f.w : f.h;\n   294→      d.canvas = {\n   295→        format: fmt,\n   296→        orientation: orient,\n   297→        w, h,\n   298→        bg: args.background || d.canvas.bg,\n   299→      };\n   300→      bus.emit(\"canvas:changed\", {});\n   301→      return txt(`Canvas: ${fmt} ${orient} (${w}x${h}mm) bg=${d.canvas.bg}`);\n   302→    }\n   303→\n   304→    // ---- Elements ----\n   305→    case \"add_text\": {\n   306→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   307→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   308→      // Resolve relative positioning\n   309→      let x = args.x, y = args.y;\n   310→      if (hasRelativeArgs(args)) {\n   311→        try {\n   312→          const pos = resolvePosition(d, \"text\", args);\n   313→          if (pos.x != null) x = pos.x;\n   314→          if (pos.y != null) y = pos.y;\n   315→        } catch (e: any) {\n   316→          return txt(`Position error: ${e.message}`);\n   317→        }\n   318→      }\n   319→      if (x == null || y == null) return txt(\"Missing coordinates: provide x/y or use relative positioning (below/above/right_of/left_of/center_h/center_v)\");\n   320→      const eid = genId();\n   321→      const newEl = {\n   322→        id: eid,\n   323→        name: args.name || undefined,\n   324→        type: \"text\",\n   325→        x, y,\n   326→        text: args.text,\n   327→        fontSize: args.fontSize ?? 8,\n   328→        fontFamily: args.fontFamily ?? \"Libre Baskerville\",\n   329→        fontWeight: args.fontWeight ?? \"bold\",\n   330→        fontStyle: args.fontStyle ?? \"normal\",\n   331→        fill:     }\n   359→      }\n   360→      if (x == null || y == null) return txt(\"Missing coordinates: provide x/y or use relative positioning (below/above/right_of/left_of/center_h/center_v)\");\n   361→      const eid = genId();\n   362→      const dims = getImageDimensions(args.path);\n   363→      const newEl = {\n   364→        id: eid,\n   365→        name: args.name || undefined,\n   366→        type: \"image\",\n   367→        x, y,\n   368→        width: args.width,\n   369→        height: args.height,\n   370→        path: args.path,\n   371→        href,\n   372→        preserveAspectRatio: args.preserveAspectRatio ?? \"xMidYMid slice\",\n   373→        naturalWidth: dims?.w ?? args.width,\n   374→        naturalHeight: dims?.h ?? args.height,\n   375→        objectFit: args.objectFit ?? \"cover\",\n   376→        cropX: args.cropX ?? 0.5,\n   377→        cropY: args.cropY ?? 0.5,\n   378→        cropZoom: args.cropZoom ?? 1,\n   379→        flipH: args.flipH ?? false,\n   380→        flipV: args.flipV ?? false,\n   381→        opacity: args.opacity ?? 1,\n   382→        rotation: args.rotation ?? 0,\n   383→        brightness: args.brightness ?? 100,\n   384→        contrast: args.contrast ?? 100,\n   385→        grayscale: args.grayscale ?? 0,\n   386→        borderWidth: args.borderWidth ?? 0,\n   387→        borderColor: (below/above/right_of/left_of/center_h/center_v)\");\n   414→      const eid = genId();\n   415→      const newEl = {\n   416→        id: eid,\n   417→        name: args.name || undefined,\n   418→   449→      }\n   450→      const eid = genId();\n   451→      const newEl = {\n   452→        id: eid,\n   453→        name: args.name || undefined,\n   454→        type: \"line\",\n   455→        x1, y1, x2, y2,\n   456→        stroke: args.stroke ?? \"#000000\",\n   457→        strokeWidth: args.strokeWidth ?? 0.5,\n   458→        opacity: args.opacity ?? 1,\n   459→        rotation: bus.emit(\"element:added\", { id: eid });\n   463→      return txt(`Line → ${eid}${args.name ? ` (${args.name})` : \"\"}`);\n   464→    }\n   465→\n   466→    case \"update_element\": {\n   467→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   468→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   469→      const el = findEl(d, args.id);\n   470→      if (!el) return txt(`Not found: ${args.id}`);\n   471→      if (args.props.path && el.type === \"image\") {\n   472→        args.props.href = loadImageAsDataUri(args.props.path);\n   473→        const dims = getImageDimensions(args.props.path);\n   474→        if (dims) {\n   475→          args.props.naturalWidth = dims.w;\n   476→          args.props.naturalHeight = dims.h;\n   477→        }\n   478→      }\n   479→      Object.assign(el, args.props);\n   480→      bus.emit(\"element:updated\", { id: el.id });\n   481→      return txt(`Updated ${el.id}${el.name ? ` (${el.name})` : \"\"}`);\n   482→    }\n   483→\n   484→    case \"batch_update\": {\n   485→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   486→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   487→      if (!Array.isArray(args.updates)) return txt(\"updates must be an array\");\n   488→      let count = 0;\n   489→      for (const u of args.updates) {\n   490→        const el = findInTree(d.elements, u.id);\n   491→        if (el && u.props) {\n   492→          if (u.props.path && el.type === \"image\") {\n   493→            u.props.href = loadImageAsDataUri(u.props.path);\n   494→            const dims = getImageDimensions(u.props.path);\n   495→            if (dims) { u.props.naturalWidth = dims.w; u.props.naturalHeight = dims.h; }\n   496→          }\n   497→          Object.assign(el, u.props);\n   498→          count++;\n   499→        }\n   500→      }\n   501→      bus.emit(\"element:updated\", { id: \"batch\" });\n   502→      return txt(`Batch updated ${count}/${args.updates.length} elements`);\n   503→    }\n   504→\n   505→    case \"delete_element\": {\n   506→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   507→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   508→      const found = findInTreeWithParent(d.elements, args.id);\n   509→      if (!found) return txt(`Not found: ${args.id}`);\n   510→      const removed = found.parent.splice(found.index, 1)[0];\n   511→      const childCount = removed.type === \"group\" ? countElements((removed as GroupElement).children) : 0;\n   512→      bus.emit(\"element:deleted\", { id: removed.id });\n   513→      const msg = `Deleted ${removed.id}${removed.name ? ` (${removed.name})` : \"\"}`;\n   514→      return txt(childCount > 0 ? `${msg} (group with ${childCount} children)` : msg);\n   515→    }\n   516→\n   517→    case \"reorder_element\": {\n   518→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   519→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   520→      const found = findInTreeWithParent(d.elements, args.id);\n   521→      if (!found) return txt(`Not found: ${args.id}`);\n   522→      const { parent, index: i } = found;\n   523→      const action = args.action;\n   524→      // Validate action before mutating\n   525→      const validActions = [\"to_front\", \"to_back\", \"forward\", \"backward\"];\n   526→      if (!validActions.includes(action)) return txt(`Invalid action: ${action}`);\n   527→      const el = parent.splice(i, 1)[0];\n   528→      switch (action) {\n   529→        case \"to_front\":\n   530→          parent.push(el);\n   531→          break;\n   532→        case \"to_back\":\n   533→          parent.unshift(el);\n   534→          break;\n   535→        case \"forward\":\n   536→          parent.splice(Math.min(i + 1, parent.length), 0, el);\n   537→          break;\n   538→        case \"backward\":\n   539→          parent.splice(Math.max(i - 1, 0), 0, el);\n   540→          break;\n   541→      }\n   542→      bus.emit(\"element:reordered\", { id: args.id, action });\n   543→      return txt(`Reordered ${args.id} → ${action}`);\n   544→    }\n   545→\n   546→    // ---- Align & Distribute ----\n   547→    case \"align\": {\n   548→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   549→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   550→      if (!Array.isArray(args.ids) || args.ids.length < 2) return txt(\"align requires at least 2 element IDs\");\n   551→      try {\n   552→        const deltas = computeAlign(d, { ids: args.ids, axis: args.axis });\n   553→        for (const delta of deltas) {\n   554→          const el = findInTree(d.elements, delta.id);\n   555→          if (el) Object.assign(el, delta.props);\n   556→        }\n   557→        if (deltas.length > 0) bus.emit(\"element:updated\", { id: \"batch\" });\n   558→        return txt(`Aligned ${args.ids.length} elements on ${args.axis} (${deltas.length} moved)`);\n   559→      } catch (e: any) {\n   560→        return txt(`Align error: ${e.message}`);\n   561→      }\n   562→    }\n   563→\n   564→    case \"distribute\": {\n   565→      const d = opentype.Font>();\n    13→\n    14→export function loadFonts(): void {\n    15→  const entries = [\n    16→    { family: \"Libre Baskerville\", weight: \"normal\", style: \"normal\", file: \"LibreBaskerville[wght].ttf\" },\n    17→    { family: \"Libre Baskerville\", weight: \"bold\", style: \"normal\", file: \"LibreBaskerville[wght].ttf\" },\n    18→    { family: \"Libre Baskerville\", weight: \"normal\", style: \"italic\", file: \"LibreBaskerville-Italic[wght].ttf\" },\n    19→    { family: \"Libre Baskerville\", weight: \"bold\", style: \"italic\", file: \"LibreBaskerville-Italic[wght].ttf\" },\n    20→    { family: \"Source Sans 3\", weight: \"normal\", style: \"normal\", file: \"SourceSans3[wght].ttf\" },\n    21→    { family: \"Source Sans 3\", weight: \"300\", style: \"normal\", file: \"SourceSans3[wght].ttf\" },\n    22→    { family: \"Source Sans 3\", weight: \"600\", style: \"normal\", file: \"SourceSans3[wght].ttf\" },\n    23→    { \"SourceSans3[wght].ttf\" },\n    25→    { family: \"Source Sans 3\", weight: \"normal\", style: \"italic\", file: \"SourceSans3-Italic[wght].ttf\" },\n    26→  ];\n    27→  const fileCache = new Map<string, opentype.Font>();\n    28→  for (const e of entries) {\n    29→    const fp = join(FONTS_DIR, e.file);\n    30→    if (!existsSync(fp)) { log(`Font not found: ${fp}`); continue; }\n    31→    try {\n    32→      if (!fileCache.has(e.file)) {\n    33→        fileCache.set(e.file, opentype.loadSync(fp));\n    34→      }\n    35→      fontMap.set(`${e.family}|${e.weight}|${e.style}`, fileCache.get(e.file)!);\n    36→    } catch (err: any) {\n    37→      log(`Failed to load font ${e.file}: ${err.message}`);\n    38→    }\n    39→  }\n    40→  log(`Loaded ${fontMap.size} font entries (${fileCache.size} files)`);\n    41→}\n    42→\n    43→export function getFont(fontFamily?: string, fontWeight?: string, fontStyle?: string): opentype.Font | null {\n    44→  const key = `${fontFamily || \"Libre Baskerville\"}|${fontWeight || \"normal\"}|${fontStyle || \"normal\"}`;\n    45→  return fontMap.get(key) || fontMap.values().next().value || null;\n    46→}\n    47→\n    48→export function measureTextWidth(text: string, fontSize: number, fontFamily?: string, fontWeight?: string, fontStyle?: string): number {\n    49→  const font = getFont(fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle);\n    50→  if (!font) return text.length * fontSize * 0.55;\n    51→  return font.getAdvanceWidth(text, fontSize);\n    52→}\n    53→\n    54→export function wrapText(text: string, maxWidth: number | null, fontSize: number, fontFamily?: string, fontWeight?: string, fontStyle?: string): string[] {\n    55→  if (!maxWidth) return text.split(\"\\n\");\n    56→  const paragraphs = text.split(\"\\n\");\n    57→  const lines: string[] = [];\n    58→  for (const para of paragraphs) {\n    59→    const words = para.split(/\\s+/).filter(Boolean);\n    60→    if (!words.length) { lines.push(\"\"); continue; }\n    61→    let cur = words[0];\n    62→    for (let i = 1; i < words.length; i++) {\n    63→      const test = cur + \" \" + words[i];\n    64→      if (measureTextWidth(test, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle) <= maxWidth) {\n    65→        cur = test;\n    66→      } else {\n    67→        lines.push(cur);\n    68→        cur = words[i];\n    69→      }\n    70→    }\n    71→    lines.push(cur);\n    72→  }\n    73→  return lines;\n    74→}\n 8;\n    42→  const fontFamily = args.fontFamily ?? \"Libre Baskerville\";\n    43→  const fontWeight = args.fontWeight ?? \"bold\";\n    44→  const fontStyle = args.fontStyle ?? \"normal\";\n    45→  const maxWidth = args.maxWidth ?? null;\n    46→  const lines = wrapText(args.text, maxWidth, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle);\n    47→  const tw = Math.max(\n    48→    ...lines.map((l) => measureTextWidth(l, fontSize, fontFamily, fontWeight, fontStyle)),\n    49→  );\n    50→  const th = fontSize * lines.length * 1.3;\n    51→  return { w: tw, h: th };\n    52→}\n    53→\n    54→/**\n    55→ * Resolve relative positioning params into concrete x/y values.\n    56→ * Returns resolved coordinates to merge into the element args.\n    57→ * Throws on errors (missing reference, no coordinates resolved).\n    58→ */\n    59→export function resolvePosition(\n    60→  doc: Document,\n    61→  type: string,\n    62→  args: any,\n    63→): ResolvedPos {\n    64→  const rel: RelativeArgs = {\n    65→    below: args.below,\n    66→    above: args.above,\n    67→    right_of: args.right_of,\n    68→    left_of: args.left_of,\n    69→    gap: args.gap ?? 0,\n    70→    center_h: args.center_h,\n    71→    center_v: args.center_v,\n    72→  };\n    73→\n    74→  const gap = rel.gap!;\n    75→  const canvas = doc.canvas;\n    76→  const result: ResolvedPos = {};\n    77→  const isLine = type === \"line\";\n    78→  const hasRelative = rel.below || rel.above || rel.right_of || rel.left_of;\n    79→\n    80→  // Get reference element bbox if relative positioning is used\n    81→  let refBox: BBox | undefined;\n    82→  let refEl: Element | undefined;\n    83→  const refName = rel.below || rel.above || rel.right_of || rel.left_of;\n    84→  if (refName) {\n    85→    refEl = findRef(doc, refName);\n    86→    if (!refEl) throw new Error(`Reference element not found: \"${refName}\"`);\n    87→    refBox = bbox(refEl);\n    88→  }\n    89→\n    90→  // ---- Vertical axis (below / above) ----\n    91→  if (rel.below && refBox) {\n    92→    const targetY = refBox.y + refBox.h + gap;\n    93→    if (isLine) {\n    94→      // offset y1/y2\n    95→      result.y1 = targetY + (args.y1 ?? 0);\n    96→      result.y2 = targetY + (args.y2 ?? 0);\n    97→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n    98→      // text y is baseline: add fontSize*0.85\n    99→      result.y = targetY + (args.fontSize ?? 8) * 0.85;\n   100→    } else {\n   101→      result.y = targetY;\n   102→    }\n   103→  }\n   104→\n   105→  if (rel.above && refBox) {\n   106→    if (isLine) {\n   107→      const lineH = Math.abs((args.y2 ?? 0) - (args.y1 ?? 0));\n   108→      const targetY = refBox.y - gap - lineH;\n   109→      result.y1 = targetY + (args.y1 ?? 0);\n   110→      result.y2 = targetY + (args.y2 ?? 0);\n   111→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   112→      // text: y is baseline, place so bottom of text aligns above ref\n   113→      result.y = refBox.y - gap;\n   114→    } else {\n   115→      // rect/image: place so bottom edge is at ref.y - gap\n   116→      const h = args.height ?? 0;\n   117→      result.y = refBox.y - gap - h;\n   118→    }\n   119→  }\n   120→\n   121→  // ---- Horizontal axis (right_of / left_of) ----\n   122→  if (rel.right_of && refBox) {\n   123→    const targetX = refBox.x + refBox.w + gap;\n   124→    if (isLine) {\n   125→      result.x1 = targetX + (args.x1 ?? 0);\n   126→      result.x2 = targetX + (args.x2 ?? 0);\n   127→    } else {\n   128→      result.x = targetX;\n   129→    }\n   130→  }\n   131→\n   132→  if (rel.left_of && refBox) {\n   133→    if (isLine) {\n   134→      const lineW = Math.abs((args.x2 ?? 0) - (args.x1 ?? 0));\n   135→      const targetX = refBox.x - gap - lineW;\n   136→      result.x1 = targetX + (args.x1 ?? 0);\n   137→      result.x2 = targetX + (args.x2 ?? 0);\n   138→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   139→      // text width depends on anchor\n   140→      const dims = textDims(args);\n   141→      const anchor = args.textAnchor ?? \"start\";\n   142→      if (anchor === \"end\") {\n   143→        result.x = refBox.x - gap;\n   144→      } else if (anchor === \"middle\") {\n   145→        result.x = refBox.x - gap - dims.w / 2;\n   146→      } else {\n   147→        result.x = refBox.x - gap - dims.w;\n   148→      }\n   149→    } else {\n   150→      const w = args.width ?? 0;\n   151→      result.x = refBox.x - gap - w;\n   152→    }\n   153→  }\n   154→\n   155→  // ---- Inherit orthogonal axis from reference ----\n   156→  if (refBox && refEl) {\n   157→    if ((rel.below || rel.above) && result.x == null && args.x == null && !rel.center_h && !isLine) {\n   158→      // Inherit x from reference element\n   159→      if (type === \"text\" && \"x\" in refEl) {\n   160→        result.x = (refEl as any).x;\n   161→      } else if (\"x\" in refEl) {\n   162→        result.x = (refEl as any).x;\n   163→      } else {\n   164→        result.x = refBox.x;\n   165→      }\n   166→    }\n   167→    if ((rel.right_of || rel.left_of) && result.y == null && args.y == null && !rel.center_v && !isLine) {\n   168→      // Inherit y from reference element\n   169→      if (\"y\" in refEl) {\n   170→        result.y = (refEl as any).y;\n   171→      } else {\n   172→        result.y = refBox.y;\n   173→      }\n   174→    }\n   175→    // For lines: inherit orthogonal axis as offset\n   176→    if (isLine && (rel.below || rel.above) && result.x1 == null && args.x1 == null) {\n   177→      if (\"x1\" in refEl) {\n   178→        result.x1 = (refEl as any).x1;\n   179→        result.x2 = (refEl as any).x2;\n   180→      } else {\n   181→        result.x1 = refBox.x;\n   182→        result.x2 = refBox.x + refBox.w;\n   183→      }\n   184→    }\n   185→    if (isLine && (rel.right_of || rel.left_of) && result.y1 == null && args.y1 == null) {\n   186→      if (\"y1\" in refEl) {\n   187→        result.y1 = (refEl as any).y1;\n   188→        result.y2 = (refEl as any).y2;\n   189→      } else {\n   190→        result.y1 = refBox.y;\n   191→        result.y2 = refBox.y + refBox.h;\n   192→      }\n   193→    }\n   194→  }\n   195→\n   196→  // ---- Canvas centering ----\n   197→  if (rel.center_h) {\n   198→    if (isLine) {\n   199→      const x1 = result.x1 ?? args.x1 ?? 0;\n   200→      const x2 = result.x2 ?? args.x2 ?? 0;\n   201→      const lineW = Math.abs(x2 - x1);\n   202→      const offset = (canvas.w - lineW) / 2 - Math.min(x1, x2);\n   203→      result.x1 = x1 + offset;\n   204→      result.x2 = x2 + offset;\n   205→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   206→      const anchor = args.textAnchor ?? \"start\";\n   207→      if (anchor === \"middle\") {\n   208→        result.x = canvas.w / 2;\n   209→      } else if (anchor === \"end\") {\n   210→        const dims = textDims(args);\n   211→        result.x = canvas.w / 2 + dims.w / 2;\n   212→      } else {\n   213→        const dims = textDims(args);\n   214→        result.x = (canvas.w - dims.w) / 2;\n   215→      }\n   216→    } else {\n   217→      const w = args.width ?? 0;\n   218→      result.x = (canvas.w - w) / 2;\n   219→    }\n   220→  }\n   221→\n   222→  if (rel.center_v) {\n   223→    if (isLine) {\n   224→      const y1 = result.y1 ?? args.y1 ?? 0;\n   225→      const y2 = result.y2 ?? args.y2 ?? 0;\n   226→      const lineH = Math.abs(y2 - y1);\n   227→      const offset = (canvas.h - lineH) / 2 - Math.min(y1, y2);\n   228→      result.y1 = y1 + offset;\n   229→      result.y2 = y2 + offset;\n   230→    } else if (type === \"text\") {\n   231→      const dims = textDims(args);\n   232→      result.y = (canvas.h - dims.h) / 2 + (args.fontSize ?? 8) * 0.85;\n   233→    } else {\n   234→      const h = args.height ?? 0;\n   235→      result.y = (canvas.h - h) / 2;\n   236→    }\n   237→  }\n   238→\n   239→  // ---- Explicit args always win ----\n   240→  // For non-line types, if x or y was explicitly provided and no relative override happened,\n   241→  // keep them. The caller should merge result over args, so we only set result if computed.\n   242→  // For lines: explicit x1/y1/x2/y2 are kept unless overridden above.\n   243→\n   244→  return result;\n   245→}\n   246→\n   247→/**\n   248→ * Check if relative positioning args are present\n   249→ */\n   250→export function hasRelativeArgs(args: any): boolean {\n   251→  return !!(args.below || args.above || args.right_of || args.left_of || args.center_h || args.center_v);\n   252→}\n   253→\n   254→// ---- Align ----\n   255→\n   256→type AlignAxis = \"left\" | \"center_h\" | \"right\" | \"top\" | \"center_v\" | \"bottom\";\n   257→\n   258→interface AlignArgs {\n   259→  ids: string[];\n   260→  axis: AlignAxis;\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→interface ElementDelta {\n   264→  id: string;\n   265→  props: Record<string, number>;\n   266→}\n   267→\n   268→export function computeAlign(doc: Document, args: AlignArgs): ElementDelta[] {\n   269→  const elements = args.ids.map((idOrName) => {\n   270→    const el = findRef(doc, idOrName);\n   271→    if (!el) throw new Error(`Element not found: \"${idOrName}\"`);\n   272→    return el;\n   273→  });\n   274→\n   275→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   276→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   277→\n   278→  switch (args.axis) {\n   279→    case \"left\": {\n   280→      const target = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x));\n   281→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   282→        const dx = target - box.x;\n   283→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   284→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   285→      }\n   286→      break;\n   287→    }\n   288→    case \"right\": {\n   289→      const target = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x + b.box.w));\n   290→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   291→        const dx = target - (box.x + box.w);\n   292→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   293→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   294→      }\n   295→      break;\n   296→    }\n   297→    case \"center_h\": {\n   298→      const minX = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x));\n   299→      const maxR = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.x + b.box.w));\n   300→      const center = (minX + maxR) / 2;\n   301→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   302→        const elCenter = box.x + box.w / 2;\n   303→        const dx = center - elCenter;\n   304→        if (Math.abs(dx) < 0.01) continue;\n   305→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   306→      }\n   307→      break;\n   308→    }\n   309→    case \"top\": {\n   310→      const target = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y));\n   311→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   312→        const dy = target - box.y;\n   313→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   314→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   315→      }\n   316→      break;\n   317→    }\n   318→    case \"bottom\": {\n   319→      const target = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y + b.box.h));\n   320→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   321→        const dy = target - (box.y + box.h);\n   322→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   323→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   324→      }\n   325→      break;\n   326→    }\n   327→    case \"center_v\": {\n   328→      const minY = Math.min(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y));\n   329→      const maxB = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.y + b.box.h));\n   330→      const center = (minY + maxB) / 2;\n   331→      for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   332→        const elCenter = box.y + box.h / 2;\n   333→        const dy = center - elCenter;\n   334→        if (Math.abs(dy) < 0.01) continue;\n   335→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   336→      }\n   337→      break;\n   338→    }\n   339→  }\n   340→\n   341→  return deltas;\n   342→}\n   343→\n   344→// ---- Distribute ----\n   345→\n   346→interface DistributeArgs {\n   347→  ids: string[];\n   348→  axis?: \"x\" | \"y\";\n   349→  gap?: number;\n   350→  grid?: {\n   351→    cols: number;\n   352→    col_gap: number;\n   353→    row_gap: number;\n   354→    start_x?: number;\n   355→    start_y?: number;\n   356→  };\n   357→}\n   358→\n   359→export function computeDistribute(doc: Document, args: DistributeArgs): ElementDelta[] {\n   360→  const elements = args.ids.map((idOrName) => {\n   361→    const el = findRef(doc, idOrName);\n   362→    if (!el) throw new Error(`Element not found: \"${idOrName}\"`);\n   363→    return el;\n   364→  });\n   365→\n   366→  if (args.grid) {\n   367→    return distributeGrid(elements, args.grid);\n   368→  }\n   369→\n   370→  const axis = args.axis ?? \"y\";\n   371→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   372→\n   373→  // Sort by position on axis\n   374→  boxes.sort((a, b) =>\n   375→    axis === \"x\" ? a.box.x - b.box.x : a.box.y - b.box.y,\n   376→  );\n   377→\n   378→  const n = boxes.length;\n   379→  if (n < 2) return [];\n   380→\n   381→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   382→\n   383→  if (axis === \"x\") {\n   384→    const totalSize = boxes.reduce((s, b) => s + b.box.w, 0);\n   385→    let gap: number;\n   386→    let startX: number;\n   387→\n   388→    if (args.gap != null) {\n   389→      gap = args.gap;\n   390→      startX = boxes[0].box.x;\n   391→    } else {\n   392→      const extent = boxes[n - 1].box.x + boxes[n - 1].box.w - boxes[0].box.x;\n   393→      gap = (extent - totalSize) / (n - 1);\n   394→      startX = boxes[0].box.x;\n   395→    }\n   396→\n   397→    let currentX = startX;\n   398→    for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   399→      const dx = currentX - box.x;\n   400→      if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) {\n   401→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, 0));\n   402→      }\n   403→      currentX += box.w + gap;\n   404→    }\n   405→  } else {\n   406→    const totalSize = boxes.reduce((s, b) => s + b.box.h, 0);\n   407→    let gap: number;\n   408→    let startY: number;\n   409→\n   410→    if (args.gap != null) {\n   411→      gap = args.gap;\n   412→      startY = boxes[0].box.y;\n   413→    } else {\n   414→      const extent = boxes[n - 1].box.y + boxes[n - 1].box.h - boxes[0].box.y;\n   415→      gap = (extent - totalSize) / (n - 1);\n   416→      startY = boxes[0].box.y;\n   417→    }\n   418→\n   419→    let currentY = startY;\n   420→    for (const { el, box } of boxes) {\n   421→      const dy = currentY - box.y;\n   422→      if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   423→        deltas.push(applyDelta(el, 0, dy));\n   424→      }\n   425→      currentY += box.h + gap;\n   426→    }\n   427→  }\n   428→\n   429→  return deltas;\n   430→}\n   431→\n   432→function distributeGrid(\n   433→  elements: Element[],\n   434→  grid: { cols: number; col_gap: number; row_gap: number; start_x?: number; start_y?: number },\n   435→): ElementDelta[] {\n   436→  const boxes = elements.map((el) => ({ el, box: bbox(el) }));\n   437→  const startX = grid.start_x ?? boxes[0].box.x;\n   438→  const startY = grid.start_y ?? boxes[0].box.y;\n   439→\n   440→  // Compute max dimensions per column and row for uniform grid\n   441→  const cols = grid.cols;\n   442→  const maxColW = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.w));\n   443→  const maxRowH = Math.max(...boxes.map((b) => b.box.h));\n   444→\n   445→  const deltas: ElementDelta[] = [];\n   446→\n   447→  for (let i = 0; i < boxes.length; i++) {\n   448→    const col = i % cols;\n   449→    const row = Math.floor(i / cols);\n   450→    const targetX = startX + col * (maxColW + grid.col_gap);\n   451→    const targetY = startY + row * (maxRowH + grid.row_gap);\n   452→\n   453→    const { el, box } = boxes[i];\n   454→    const dx = targetX - box.x;\n   455→    const dy = targetY - box.y;\n   456→\n   457→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01 || Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   458→      deltas.push(applyDelta(el, dx, dy));\n   459→    }\n   460→  }\n   461→\n   462→  return deltas;\n   463→}\n   464→\n   465→// ---- Shared: apply delta to raw coordinates ----\n   466→\n   467→function applyDelta(el: Element, dx: number, dy: number): ElementDelta {\n   468→  const props: Record<string, number> = {};\n   469→  if (el.type === \"line\") {\n   470→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) {\n   471→      props.x1 = r(el.x1 + dx);\n   472→      props.x2 = r(el.x2 + dx);\n   473→    }\n   474→    if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) {\n   475→      props.y1 = r(el.y1 + dy);\n   476→      props.y2 = r(el.y2 + dy);\n   477→    }\n   478→  } else {\n   479→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= 0.01) props.x = r((el as any).x + dx);\n   480→    if (Math.abs(dy) >= 0.01) props.y = r((el as any).y + dy);\n   481→  }\n   482→  return { id: el.id, props };\n   483→}\n   484→\n   485→function r(v: number): number {\n   486→  return Math.round(v * 10) / 10;\n   487→}\n   488→"}]},"uuid":"1015110c-7c10-4eeb-a423-68c688ffe1b8","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:21:07.587Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"6f07953c-08f2-4a46-836a-30b9a7a95e96","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}
