bleedGroup.append('rect')\n    72→      .attr('x', bleed).attr('y', bleed)\n    73→      .attr('width', canvas.w - 2 * bleed).attr('height', canvas.h - 2 * bleed)\n    74→      .attr('fill', 'none').attr('stroke', '#ff0000').attr('stroke-width', 0.3)\n    75→      .attr('stroke-dasharray', '2,2').attr('opacity', 0.4);\n    76→  }\n    77→\n    78→  elements.forEach((el: Element) => renderElement(svg, defs, el));\n    79→\n    80→  // Flatten for inspector/selection (need leaf elements from inside groups)\n    81→  const leaves = flattenLeaves(elements);\n    82→\n    83→  // Inspector overlay (bounding boxes + name labels) — hidden during drag\n    84→  if (ui.showNames && store.state.phase !== 'dragging') {\n    85→    const overlay = svg.append('g').attr('class', 'inspector-overlay').style('pointer-events', 'none');\n    86→    leaves.forEach((el: Element) => renderInspectorBox(overlay, el));\n    87→  }\n    88→\n    89→  for (const selId of ui.selectedIds) {\n    90→    const sel = findInElements(elements, selId);\n    91→    if (sel) renderSelection(svg, sel);\n    92→  }\n    93→}\n    94→\n    95→\n    96→function renderElement(svg: any, defs: any, el: Element): void {\n    97→  // Groups: recurse into children\n    98→  if (el.type === 'group') {\n    99→    const groupG = svg.append('g').attr('data-group', el.id);\n   100→    if ((el.opacity ?? 1) < 1) groupG.attr('opacity', el.opacity);\n   101→    for (const child of el.children) {\n   102→      renderElement(groupG, defs, child);\n   103→    }\n   104→    return;\n   105→  }\n   106→\n   107→  const opacity = el.opacity ?? 1;\n   108→  const rotation = el.rotation ?? 0;\n   109→\n   110→  // Create SVG filter for images with effects\n   111→  if (el.type === 'image') {\n   112→    const hasFilter = (el.brightness ?? 100) !== 100 || (el.contrast ?? 100) !== 100 || (el.grayscale ?? 0) > 0;\n   113→    const hasShadow = (el.shadowBlur > 0 || el.shadowX || el.shadowY);\n   114→\n   115→    if (hasFilter || hasShadow) {\n   116→      const filter = defs.append('filter').attr('id', `f_${el.id}`)\n   117→        .attr('x', '-20%').attr('y', '-20%').attr('width', '140%').attr('height', '140%');\n   118→      let input = 'SourceGraphic';\n   119→      if (hasShadow) {\n   120→        filter.append('feDropShadow')\n   121→          .attr('dx', el.shadowX || 0).attr('dy', el.shadowY || 0)\n   122→          .attr('stdDeviation', el.shadowBlur || 0)\n   123→          .attr('flood-color', el.shadowColor || 'rgba(0,0,0,0.4)')\n   124→          .attr('flood-opacity', 1)\n   125→          .attr('result', 'shadow');\n   126→        input = 'shadow';\n   127→      }\n   128→      if (hasFilter) {\n   129→        const sat = 1 - (el.grayscale ?? 0) / 100;\n   130→        filter.append('feColorMatrix')\n   131→          .attr('type', 'saturate').attr('values', sat)\n   132→          .attr('in', input).attr('result', 'gray');\n   133→        const b = (el.brightness ?? 100) / 100;\n   134→        const c = (el.contrast ?? 100) / 100;\n   135→        const ic = (1 - c) * 0.5;\n   136→        const ct = filter.append('feComponentTransfer').attr('in', 'gray');\n   137→        ct.append('feFuncR').attr('type', 'linear').attr('slope', b * c).attr('intercept', ic);\n   138→        ct.append('feFuncG').attr('type', 'linear').attr('slope', b * c).attr('intercept', ic);\n   139→        ct.append('feFuncB').attr('type', 'linear').attr('slope', b * c).attr('intercept', ic);\n   140→      }\n   141→    }\n   142→\n   143→    // Crop clip path for cover mode\n   144→    const fit = el.objectFit || 'cover';\n   145→    if (fit === 'cover') {\n   146→      const cp = defs.append('clipPath').attr('id', `c_${el.id}`);\n   147→      if (el.borderRadius > 0) {\n   148→        cp.append('rect').attr('x', el.x).attr('y', el.y)\n   149→          .attr('width', el.width).attr('height', el.height)\n   150→          .attr('rx', el.borderRadius);\n   151→      } else {\n   152→        cp.append('rect').attr('x', el.x).attr('y', el.y)\n   153→          .attr('width', el.width).attr('height', el.height);\n   154→      }\n   155→    }\n   156→  }\n   157→\n   158→  // Wrap in group for transforms\n   159→  const g = svg.append('g');\n   160→  if (opacity < 1) g.attr('opacity', opacity);\n   161→  if (rotation !== 0) {\n   162→    let cx: number, cy: number;\n   163→    if (el.type === 'line') {\n   164→      cx = (el.x1 + el.x2) / 2; cy = (el.y1 + el.y2) / 2;\n   165→    } else if (el.type === 'text') {\n   166→      cx = el.x; cy = el.y;\n   167→    } else {\n   168→      cx = el.x + ((el as any).width || 0) / 2; cy = el.y + ((el as any).height || 0) / 2;\n   169→    }\n   170→    g.attr('transform', `rotate(${rotation}, ${cx}, ${cy})`);\n   171→  }\n   172→\n   173→  let node: any;\n   174→\n   175→  switch (el.type) {\n   176→    case 'rect':\n   177→      node = g.append('rect')\n   178→        .attr('x', el.x).attr('y', el.y)\n   179→        .attr('width', el.width).attr('height', el.height)\n   180→        .attr('fill', el.fill).attr('stroke', el.stroke)\n   181→        .attr('stroke-width', el.strokeWidth).attr('rx', el.rx);\n   182→      break;\n   183→\n   184→    case 'line':\n   185→      node = g.append('line')\n   186→        .attr('x1', el.x1).attr('y1', el.y1)\n   187→        .attr('x2', el.x2).attr('y2', el.y2)\n   188→        .attr('stroke', el.stroke).attr('stroke-width', el.strokeWidth);\n   189→      break;\n   190→\n   191→    case 'image': {\n   192→      const hasFilter = (el.brightness ?? 100) !== 100 || (el.contrast ?? 100) !== 100 || (el.grayscale ?? 0) > 0;\n   193→      const hasShadow = (el.shadowBlur > 0 || el.shadowX || el.shadowY);\n   194→      const filterAttr = (hasFilter || hasShadow) ? `url(#f_${el.id})` : null;\n   195→      const fit = el.objectFit || 'cover';\n   196→\n   197→      // Flip transform string (applied around frame center)\n   198→      const flipH = el.flipH ? -1 : 1, flipV = el.flipV ? -1 : 1;\n   199→      const needFlip = flipH === -1 || flipV === -1;\n   200→      const fcx = el.x + el.width / 2, fcy = el.y + el.height / 2;\n   201→      const flipTransform = needFlip\n   202→        ? `translate(${fcx},${fcy}) scale(${flipH},${flipV}) translate(${-fcx},${-fcy})`\n   203→        : '';\n   204→\n   205→      if (fit === 'cover' && el.naturalWidth > 0 && el.naturalHeight > 0) {\n   206→        // Cover: scale image to fill frame, crop with clipPath, position via cropX/cropY\n   207→        const frameW = el.width, frameH = el.height;\n   208→        const natW = el.naturalWidth, natH = el.naturalHeight;\n   209→        const zoom = el.cropZoom || 1;\n   210→        const baseScale = Math.max(frameW / natW, frameH / natH);\n   211→        const scale = baseScale * zoom;\n   212→        const imgW = natW * scale, imgH = natH * scale;\n   213→        const cropX = el.cropX ?? 0.5, cropY = el.cropY ?? 0.5;\n   214→        const imgX = el.x - (imgW - frameW) * cropX;\n   215→        const imgY = el.y - (imgH - frameH) * cropY;\n   216→\n   217→        const imgG = g.append('g')\n   218→          .attr('clip-path', `url(#c_${el.id})`)\n   219→          .style('pointer-events', 'none');\n   220→        if (flipTransform) imgG.attr('transform', flipTransform);\n   221→\n   222→        const img = imgG.append('image')\n   223→          .attr('x', imgX).attr('y', imgY)\n   224→          .attr('width', imgW).attr('height', imgH)\n   225→          .attr('href', el.href)\n   226→          .attr('preserveAspectRatio', 'none');\n   227→        if (filterAttr) img.attr('filter', filterAttr);\n   228→\n   229→        // Transparent hit rect for interaction (drag moves this rect; image re-renders on state update)\n   230→        node = g.append('rect')\n   231→          .attr('x', el.x).attr('y', el.y)\n   232→          .attr('width', el.width).attr('height', el.height)\n   233→          .attr('fill', 'transparent');\n   234→\n   235→      } else if (fit === 'contain') {\n   236→        // Contain: fit inside frame, no clip\n   237→        if (flipTransform) {\n   238→          g.attr('transform', (g.attr('transform') || '') + ' ' + flipTransform);\n   239→        }\n   240→        node = g.append('image')\n   241→          .attr('x', el.x).attr('y', el.y)\n   242→          .attr('width', el.width).attr('height', el.height)\n   243→          .attr('href', el.href)\n   244→          .attr('preserveAspectRatio', 'xMidYMid meet');\n   245→        if (filterAttr) node.attr('filter', filterAttr);\n   246→\n   247→      } else {\n   248→        // Fill: stretch to fit, no clip\n   249→        if (flipTransform) {\n   250→          g.attr('transform', (g.attr('transform') || '') + ' ' + flipTransform);\n   251→        }\n   252→        node = g.append('image')\n   253→          .attr('x', el.x).attr('y', el.y)\n   254→          .attr('width', el.width).attr('height', el.height)\n   255→          .attr('href', el.href)\n   256→          .attr('preserveAspectRatio', 'none');\n   257→        if (filterAttr) node.attr('filter', filterAttr);\n   258→      }\n   259→\n   260→      // Border\n   261→      if (el.borderWidth > 0) {\n   262→        g.append('rect')\n   263→          .attr('x', el.x).attr('y', el.y)\n   264→          .attr('width', el.width).attr('height', el.height)\n   265→          .attr('fill', 'none')\n   266→          .attr('stroke', el.borderColor || '#000')\n   267→          .attr('stroke-width', el.borderWidth)\n   268→          .attr('rx', el.borderRadius || 0)\n   269→          .style('pointer-events', 'none');\n   270→      }\n   271→      break;\n   272→    }\n   273→\n   274→    case 'text': {\n   275→      const lines = el.maxWidth\n   276→        ? wrapTextClient(el.text, el.maxWidth, el.fontSize, el.fontFamily, el.fontWeight, el.fontStyle)\n   277→        : el.text.split('\\n');\n   278→      const lh = el.fontSize * 1.3;\n   279→      node = g.append('text')\n   280→        .attr('x', el.x).attr('y', el.y)\n   281→        .attr('font-family', el.fontFamily)\n   282→        .attr('font-size', el.fontSize)\n   283→        .attr('font-weight', el.fontWeight)\n   284→        .attr('font-style', el.fontStyle)\n   285→        .attr('fill', el.fill)\n   286→        .attr('text-anchor', el.textAnchor);\n   287→\n   288→      lines.forEach((line: string, i: number) => {\n   289→        const tspan = node.append('tspan').text(line);\n   290→        if (i > 0) { tspan.attr('x', el.x).attr('dy', lh); }\n   291→      });\n   292→\n   293→      // Visual maxWidth guide when selected\n   294→      if (el.maxWidth && store.state.ui.selectedIds.includes(el.id)) {\n   295→        const totalH = lines.length * lh;\n   296→        let gx = el.x;\n   297→        if (el.textAnchor === 'middle') gx -= el.maxWidth / 2;\n   298→        else if (el.textAnchor === 'end') gx -= el.maxWidth;\n   299→        svg.append('rect')\n   300→          .attr('class', 'maxwidth-guide')\n   301→          .attr('x', gx).attr('y', el.y - el.fontSize * 0.85)\n   302→          .attr('width', el.maxWidth).attr('height', totalH)\n   303→          .attr('fill', 'none')\n   304→          .attr('stroke', '#3B82F6').attr('stroke-width', 0.3)\n   305→          .attr('stroke-dasharray', '1.5,1')\n   306→          .style('pointer-events', 'none');\n   307→      }\n   308→      break;\n   309→    }\n   310→  }\n   311→\n   312→  if (!node) return;\n   313→\n   314→  node.attr('class', 'element').attr('data-id', el.id);\n   315→\n   316→  // Skip interaction handlers when document is locked (pan mode)\n   317→  if (store.state.ui.documentLocked) return;\n   318→\n   319→  node.on('click', (event: any) => {\n   320→    event.stopPropagation();\n   321→    const toggle = event.shiftKey || event.metaKey;\n   322→    setSelection(el.id, toggle);\n   323→  });\n   324→\n   325→  // Double-click on image opens editor modal\n   326→  if (el.type === 'image') {\n   327→    node.on('dblclick', (event: any) => {\n   328→      event.stopPropagation();\n   329→      document.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('open-image-editor', { detail: { id: el.id } }));\n   330→    });\n   331→  }\n   332→\n   333→  const dragBehavior = d3.drag()\n   334→    .on('start', function (this: any, event: any) {\n   335→      const selectedIds = store.state.ui.selectedIds;\n   336→      const isInSelection = selectedIds.includes(el.id);\n   337→\n   338→      // If dragging an element not in the selection, select it first\n   339→      if (!isInSelection) {\n   340→        setSelection(el.id);\n   341→        this._multiDrag = null;\n   342→      }\n   343→\n   344→      dispatch({ type: \"DRAG_START\", elId: el.id });\n   345→      const svgPt = toSVG(event.sourceEvent);\n   346→\n   347→      // Record primary element offset\n   348→      if (el.type === 'line') {\n   349→        this._ox1 = el.x1 - svgPt.x; this._oy1 = el.y1 - svgPt.y;\n   350→        this._ox2 = el.x2 - svgPt.x; this._oy2 = el.y2 - svgPt.y;\n   351→        this._startProps = { x1: el.x1, y1: el.y1, x2: el.x2, y2: el.y2 };\n   352→      } else {\n   353→        this._ox = (el as any).x - svgPt.x; this._oy = (el as any).y - svgPt.y;\n   354→        this._startProps = { x: (el as any).x, y: (el as any).y };\n   355→      }\n   356→\n   357→      // Multi-drag: record start positions of all OTHER selected elements\n   358→      const dragIds = isInSelection ? selectedIds : [el.id];\n   359→      if (dragIds.length > 1) {\n   360→        const doc = store.state.doc.currentDoc;\n   361→        if (doc) {\n   362→          const others: Array<{ el: Element; start: any }> = [];\n   363→          for (const sid of dragIds) {\n   364→            if (sid === el.id) continue;\n   365→            const other = findInElements(doc.elements, sid);\n   366→            if (!other) continue;\n   367→            if (other.type === 'line') {\n   368→              others.push({ el: other, start: { x1: other.x1, y1: other.y1, x2: other.x2, y2: other.y2 } });\n   369→            } else if (other.type !== 'group') {\n   370→              others.push({ el: other, start: { x: (other as any).x, y: (other as any).y } });\n   371→            }\n   372→          }\n   373→          this._multiDrag = others;\n   374→        }\n   375→      } else {\n   376→        this._multiDrag = null;\n   377→      }\n   378→\n   379→      // Pre-compute snap targets excluding all dragged elements\n   380→      const doc = store.state.doc.currentDoc;\n   381→      if (store.state.ui.snapEnabled && doc) {\n   382→        this._snapTargets = collectSnapTargets(doc.elements, new Set(dragIds), doc.canvas);\n   383→      } else {\n   384→        this._snapTargets = null;\n   385→      }\n   386→      this._guideGroup = d3.select('#canvas').append('g').attr('class', 'snap-guides').style('pointer-events', 'none');\n   387→      d3.select('.inspector-overlay').style('display', 'none');\n   388→    })\n   389→    .on('drag', function (this: any, event: any) {\n   390→      const svgPt = toSVG(event.sourceEvent);\n   391→      let dx = 0, dy = 0;\n   392→\n   393→      if (el.type === 'line') {\n   394→        let x1 = svgPt.x + this._ox1, y1 = svgPt.y + this._oy1;\n   395→        let x2 = svgPt.x + this._ox2, y2 = svgPt.y + this._oy2;\n   396→        if (this._snapTargets) {\n   397→          const lx = Math.min(x1, x2), ly = Math.min(y1, y2);\n   398→          const lw = Math.abs(x2 - x1) || 0.5, lh = Math.abs(y2 - y1) || 0.5;\n   399→          const snap = computeSnap({ x: lx, y: ly, w: lw, h: lh }, this._snapTargets);\n   400→          const sdx = snap.x - lx, sdy = snap.y - ly;\n   401→          x1 += sdx; y1 += sdy; x2 += sdx; y2 += sdy;\n   402→          dispatch({ type: \"DRAG_MOVE\", snapGuides: snap.guides });\n   403→          renderGuides(this._guideGroup, snap.guides);\n   404→        }\n   405→        dx = x1 - el.x1; dy = y1 - el.y1;\n   406→        el.x1 = x1; el.y1 = y1; el.x2 = x2; el.y2 = y2;\n   407→        d3.select(this).attr('x1', el.x1).attr('y1', el.y1).attr('x2', el.x2).attr('y2', el.y2);\n   408→      } else {\n   409→        let newX = svgPt.x + this._ox;\n   410→        let newY = svgPt.y + this._oy;\n   411→        if (this._snapTargets) {\n   412→          let bx = newX, by = newY;\n   413→          let w = (el as any).width || 0, h = (el as any).height || 0;\n   414→          if (el.type === 'text') {\n   415→            const tw = (el as any).maxWidth || (el.text.length * el.fontSize * 0.55);\n   416→            const th = el.fontSize * 1.3 * (el.text.split(\"\\n\").length);\n   417→            bx = (el as any).textAnchor === \"middle\" ? newX - tw / 2 : (el as any).textAnchor === \"end\" ? newX - tw : newX;\n   418→            by = newY - el.fontSize * 0.85;\n   419→            w = tw; h = th;\n   420→          }\n   421→          const snap = computeSnap({ x: bx, y: by, w, h }, this._snapTargets);\n   422→          newX += snap.x - bx;\n   423→          newY += snap.y - by;\n   424→          dispatch({ type: \"DRAG_MOVE\", snapGuides: snap.guides });\n   425→          renderGuides(this._guideGroup, snap.guides);\n   426→        }\n   427→        dx = newX - (el as any).x; dy = newY - (el as any).y;\n   428→        (el as any).x = newX; (el as any).y = newY;\n   429→        d3.select(this).attr('x', (el as any).x).attr('y', (el as any).y);\n   430→        if (el.type === 'text') {\n   431→          d3.select(this).selectAll('tspan')\n   432→            .filter(function (this: any) { return d3.select(this).attr('x') !== null; })\n   433→            .attr('x', (el as any).x);\n   434→        }\n   435→      }\n   436→\n   437→      // Move other selected elements by the same delta\n   438→      if (this._multiDrag && (dx !== 0 || dy !== 0)) {\n   439→        for (const { el: other } of this._multiDrag) {\n   440→          if (other.type === 'line') {\n   441→            other.x1 += dx; other.y1 += dy; other.x2 += dx; other.y2 += dy;\n   442→            const n = d3.select(`[data-id=\"${other.id}\"]`);\n   443→            n.attr('x1', other.x1).attr('y1', other.y1).attr('x2', other.x2).attr('y2', other.y2);\n   444→          } else if (other.type !== 'group') {\n   445→            (other as any).x += dx; (other as any).y += dy;\n   446→            const n = d3.select(`[data-id=\"${other.id}\"]`);\n   447→            n.attr('x', (other as any).x).attr('y', (other as any).y);\n   448→            if (other.type === 'text') {\n   449→              n.selectAll('tspan')\n   450→                .filter(function (this: any) { return d3.select(this).attr('x') !== null; })\n   451→                .attr('x', (other as any).x);\n   452→            }\n   453→          }\n   454→        }\n   455→      }\n   456→\n   457→      d3.selectAll('.selection-rect').remove();\n   458→      const svg = d3.select('#canvas');\n   459→      renderSelection(svg, el);\n   460→      if (this._multiDrag) {\n   461→        for (const { el: other } of this._multiDrag) renderSelection(svg, other);\n   462→      }\n   463→    })\n   464→    .on('end', function (this: any) {\n   465→      dispatch({ type: \"DRAG_END\" });\n   466→      this._guideGroup?.remove();\n   467→      d3.select('.inspector-overlay').style('display', null);\n   468→\n   469→      // Collect all undo/redo entries\n   470→      const undoEntries: Array<{ id: string; oldProps: any; newProps: any }> = [];\n   471→\n   472→      if (el.type === 'line') {\n   473→        const newProps = { x1: r(el.x1), y1: r(el.y1), x2: r(el.x2), y2: r(el.y2) };\n   474→        undoEntries.push({ id: el.id, oldProps: this._startProps, newProps });\n   475→        sendUpdate(el.id, newProps);\n   476→      } else {\n   477→        const newProps = { x: r((el as any).x), y: r((el as any).y) };\n   478→        undoEntries.push({ id: el.id, oldProps: this._startProps, newProps });\n   479→        sendUpdate(el.id, newProps);\n   480→      }\n   481→\n   482→      if (this._multiDrag) {\n   483→        for (const { el: other, start } of this._multiDrag) {\n   484→          let newProps: any;\n   485→          if (other.type === 'line') {\n   486→            newProps = { x1: r(other.x1), y1: r(other.y1), x2: r(other.x2), y2: r(other.y2) };\n   487→          } else if (other.type !== 'group') {\n   488→            newProps = { x: r((other as any).x), y: r((other as any).y) };\n   489→          }\n   490→          if (newProps) {\n   491→            undoEntries.push({ id: other.id, oldProps: start, newProps });\n   492→            sendUpdate(other.id, newProps);\n   493→          }\n   494→        }\n   495→      }\n   496→\n   497→      // Single compound undo entry\n   498→      const moved = undoEntries.filter(e => {\n   499→        const o = e.oldProps, n = e.newProps;\n   500→        return o.x !== n.x || o.y !== n.y || o.x1 !== n.x1 || o.y1 !== n.y1;\n   501→      });\n   502→      if (moved.length > 0) {\n   503→        undoManager.push({\n   504→          label: `Drag ${moved.length} element(s)`,\n   505→          undo: () => { for (const e of moved) sendUpdate(e.id, e.oldProps); },\n   506→          redo: () => { for (const e of moved) sendUpdate(e.id, e.newProps); },\n   507→        });\n   508→      }\n   509→    });\n   510→  node.call(dragBehavior);\n   511→}\n   512→\n   513→\n   514→function renderSelection(svg: any, el: Element): void {\n   515→  const bbox = elementBBox(el);\n   516→  if (!bbox) return;\n   517→  svg.append('rect').attr('class', 'selection-rect')\n   518→    .attr('x', bbox.x - 1).attr('y', bbox.y - 1)\n   519→    .attr('width', bbox.w + 2).attr('height', bbox.h + 2);\n   520→}\n   521→\n   522→function renderInspectorBox(overlay: any, el: Element): void {\n   523→  let bx: number, by: number, bw: number, bh: number;\n   524→  if (el.type === 'line') {\n   525→    bx = Math.min(el.x1, el.x2);\n   526→    by = Math.min(el.y1, el.y2);\n   527→    bw = 531→    if (textNode) {\n   532→      const b = textNode.getBBox();\n   533→      bx = b.x; by = b.y; bw = b.width; bh = b.height;\n   534→    } else {\n   535→      bx = el.x; by = el.y - el.fontSize; bw = 20; bh = el.fontSize;\n   536→    }\n   537→  } else if (el.type === 'rect' || el.type === 'image') {\n   538→    bx = el.x; by = el.y; bw = el.width; bh = el.height;\n   539→  } {"parentUuid":"f9aec51d-f28f-45b1-916c-fd793e82ae41","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"61576487-1349-4f01-9df8-d7b4fbba612a","agentId":"a792f2c641a6b23ec","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01QLxCMf6XXPWZGZtmQgjzv4","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→// ============================================================\n     2→// LAYOUT — check_layout: bbox, overlaps, bleed, spacing\n     3→// ============================================================\n     4→\n     5→import type { Document, Element, GroupElement, BBox } from \"./types.js\";\n     6→import { wrapText, measureTextWidth } from \"./fonts.js\";\n     7→import { flattenLeaves } from \"./tree.js\";\n     8→\n     9→export function bbox(el: Element): BBox {\n    10→  switch (el.type) {\n    11→    case \"rect\":\n    12→    case \"image\":\n    13→      return { x: el.x, y: el.y, w: el.width, h: el.height };\n    14→    case \"line\": {\n    15→      const x = Math.min(el.x1, el.x2), y = Math.min(el.y1, el.y2);\n    16→      return { x, y, w: Math.abs(el.x2 - el.x1) || 0.5, h: Math.abs(el.y2 - el.y1) || 0.5 };\n    17→    }\n    18→    case \"text\": {\n    19→      const lines = el.maxWidth\n    20→        ? wrapText(el.text, el.maxWidth, el.fontSize, el.fontFamily, el.fontWeight, el.fontStyle)\n    21→        : el.text.split(\"\\n\");\n    22→      const tw = el.maxWidth\n    23→        ? Math.max(...lines.map((l) => measureTextWidth(l, el.fontSize, el.fontFamily, el.fontWeight, el.fontStyle)))\n    24→        : Math.max(...lines.map((l) => l.length)) * el.fontSize * 0.55;\n    25→      const th = el.fontSize * lines.length * 1.3;\n    26→      let tx = el.x;\n    27→      if (el.textAnchor === \"middle\") tx -= tw / 2;\n    28→      else if (el.textAnchor === \"end\") tx -= tw;\n    29→      const ty = el.y - el.fontSize * 0.85;\n    30→      return { x: tx, y: ty, w: tw, h: th };\n    31→    }\n    32→    case \"group\": {\n    33→      const children = (el as GroupElement).children;\n    34→      if (!children.length) return { x: 0, y: 0, w: 0, h: 0 };\n    35→      let minX = Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;\n    36→      for (const child of children) {\n    37→        const cb = bbox(child);\n    38→        minX = Math.min(minX, cb.x);\n    39→        minY = Math.min(minY, cb.y);\n    40→        maxX = Math.max(maxX, cb.x + cb.w);\n    41→        maxY = Math.max(maxY, cb.y + cb.h);\n    42→      }\n    43→      return { x: minX, y: minY, w: maxX - minX, h: maxY - minY };\n    44→    }\n    45→    default:\n    46→      return { x: 0, y: 0, w: 0, h: 0 };\n    47→  }\n    48→}\n    49→\n    50→export interface ColorWarning {\n    51→  id: string;\n    52→  type: string;\n    53→  property: string;\n    54→  value: string;\n    55→  reason: string;\n    56→}\n    57→\n    58→export interface LayoutReport {\n    59→  structuralLayers: string[];\n    60→  overlaps: any[];\n    61→  outOfBounds: any[];\n    62→  bleedZone: any[];\n    63→  spacingGroups: any[];\n    64→  colorWarnings: ColorWarning[];\n    65→}\n    66→\n    67→export function checkLayout(\n    68→  d: Document,\n    69→  bleed: number,\n    70→  spaceTol: number,\n    71→  sizeTol: number,\n    72→): LayoutReport {\n    73→  const { w: cW, h: cH } = d.canvas;\n    74→\n    75→  const leaves = flattenLeaves(d.elements);\n    76→  const boxes = leaves.map((el) => ({ id: el.id, type: el.type, bbox: bbox(el), el }));\n    77→\n    78→  // Structural layer detection\n    79→  const canvasArea = cW * cH;\n    80→  const isStructural = (b: typeof boxes[0]) => {\n    81→    const area = b.bbox.w * b.bbox.h;\n    82→    if (area > canvasArea * 0.5) return true;\n    83→    if (b.type === \"rect\" && (b.el.opacity ?? 1) < 1 && (b.bbox.w >= cW * 0.95 || b.bbox.h >= cH * 0.95)) return true;\n    84→    return false;\n    85→  };\n    86→  const structuralIds = new Set(boxes.filter(isStructural).map((b) => b.id));\n    87→\n    88→  // 1. Pairwise overlaps (skip structural layers)\n    89→  const overlaps: any[] = [];\n    90→  for (let i = 0; i < boxes.length; i++) {\n    91→    for (let j = i + 1; j < boxes.length; j++) {\n    92→      if (structuralIds.has(boxes[i].id) || structuralIds.has(boxes[j].id)) continue;\n    93→      const a = boxes[i].bbox, b = boxes[j].bbox;\n    94→      const ix = Math.max(a.x, b.x);\n    95→      const iy = Math.max(a.y, b.y);\n    96→      const ix2 = Math.min(a.x + a.w, b.x + b.w);\n    97→      const iy2 = Math.min(a.y + a.h, b.y + b.h);\n    98→      if (ix < ix2 && iy < iy2) {\n    99→        const iw = Math.round((ix2 - ix) * 10) / 10;\n   100→        const ih = Math.round((iy2 - iy) * 10) / 10;\n   101→        overlaps.push({\n   102→          a: boxes[i].id,\n   103→          b: boxes[j].id,\n   104→          a_type: boxes[i].type,\n   105→          b_type: boxes[j].type,\n   106→          intersection: { x: Math.round(ix * 10) / 10, y: Math.round(iy * 10) / 10, w: iw, h: ih },\n   107→          area_mm2: Math.round(iw * ih * 10) / 10,\n   108→        });\n   109→      }\n   110→    }\n   111→  }\n   112→\n   113→  // 2. Out of bounds\n   114→  const outOfBounds: any[] = [];\n   115→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   116→    const { x, y, w, h } = b.bbox;\n   117→    const sides: any[] = [];\n   118→    if (x < 0) sides.push({ side: \"left\", overflow_mm: Math.round(-x * 10) / 10 });\n   119→    if (y < 0) sides.push({ side: \"top\", overflow_mm: Math.round(-y * 10) / 10 });\n   120→    if (x + w > cW) sides.push({ side: \"right\", overflow_mm: Math.round((x + w - cW) * 10) / 10 });\n   121→    if (y + h > cH) sides.push({ side: \"bottom\", overflow_mm: Math.round((y + h - cH) * 10) / 10 });\n   122→    for (const s of sides) outOfBounds.push({ id: b.id, ...s });\n   123→  }\n   124→\n   125→  // 3. Bleed zone\n   126→  const bleedZone: any[] = [];\n   127→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   128→    const { x, y, w, h } = b.bbox;\n   129→    if (w >= cW * 0.95 && h >= cH * 0.95) continue;\n   130→    const sides: any[] = [];\n   131→    if (x > 0 && x < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"left\", distance_mm: Math.round(x * 10) / 10 });\n   132→    if (y > 0 && y < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"top\", distance_mm: Math.round(y * 10) / 10 });\n   133→    if (x + w < cW && cW - (x + w) < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"right\", distance_mm: Math.round((cW - x - w) * 10) / 10 });\n   134→    if (y + h < cH && cH - (y + h) < bleed) sides.push({ side: \"bottom\", distance_mm: Math.round((cH - y - h) * 10) / 10 });\n   135→    for (const s of sides) bleedZone.push({ id: b.id, ...s });\n   136→  }\n   137→\n   138→  // 4. Spacing groups\n   139→  const spacingGroups: any[] = [];\n   140→  const sizeKey = (b: typeof boxes[0]) => `${b.type}_${Math.round(b.bbox.w / sizeTol) * sizeTol}_${Math.round(b.bbox.h / sizeTol) * sizeTol}`;\n   141→  const groups = new Map<string, typeof boxes>();\n   142→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   143→    const k = sizeKey(b);\n   144→    if (!groups.has(k)) groups.set(k, []);\n   145→    groups.get(k)!.push(b);\n   146→  }\n   147→  for (const [, members] of groups) {\n   148→    if (members.length < 3) continue;\n   149→    const ys = members.map((m) => m.bbox.y);\n   150→    const ySpread = Math.max(...ys) - Math.min(...ys);\n   151→    const xs = members.map((m) => m.bbox.x);\n   152→    const xSpread = Math.max(...xs) - Math.min(...xs);\n   153→\n   154→    if (xSpread > ySpread) {\n   155→      const sorted = [...members].sort((a, b) => a.bbox.x - b.bbox.x);\n   156→      const gaps: number[] = [];\n   157→      for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {\n   158→        gaps.push(Math.round((sorted[i].bbox.x - sorted[i - 1].bbox.x - sorted[i - 1].bbox.w) * 10) / 10);\n   159→      }\n   160→      const avgGap = gaps.reduce((s, g) => s + g, 0) / gaps.length;\n   161→      const uniform = gaps.every((g) => Math.abs(g - avgGap) <= spaceTol);\n   162→      spacingGroups.push({\n   163→        ids: sorted.map((m) => m.id),\n   164→        type: members[0].type,\n   165→        axis: \"horizontal\",\n   166→        gaps_mm: gaps,\n   167→        avg_gap_mm: Math.round(avgGap * 10) / 10,\n   168→        uniform,\n   169→      });\n   170→    } else {\n   171→      const sorted = [...members].sort((a, b) => a.bbox.y - b.bbox.y);\n   172→      const gaps: number[] = [];\n   173→      for (let i = 1; i < sorted.length; i++) {\n   174→        gaps.push(Math.round((sorted[i].bbox.y - sorted[i - 1].bbox.y - sorted[i - 1].bbox.h) * 10) / 10);\n   175→      }\n   176→      const avgGap = gaps.reduce((s, g) => s + g, 0) / gaps.length;\n   177→      const uniform = gaps.every((g) => Math.abs(g - avgGap) <= spaceTol);\n   178→      spacingGroups.push({\n   179→        ids: sorted.map((m) => m.id),\n   180→        type: members[0].type,\n   181→        axis: \"vertical\",\n   182→        gaps_mm: gaps,\n   183→        avg_gap_mm: Math.round(avgGap * 10) / 10,\n   184→        uniform,\n   185→      });\n   186→    }\n   187→  }\n   188→\n   189→  // 5. CMYK color warnings\n   190→  const colorWarnings: ColorWarning[] = [];\n   191→  for (const b of boxes) {\n   192→    const el = b.el;\n   193→    const colorProps: [string, string | undefined][] = [\n   194→      [\"fill\", (el as any).fill],\n   195→      [\"stroke\", (el as any).stroke],\n   196→      [\"borderColor\", (el as any).borderColor],\n   197→      [\"shadowColor\", (el as any).shadowColor],\n   198→    ];\n   199→    for (const [prop, val] of colorProps) {\n   200→      if (!val || val === \"none\") continue;\n   201→      if (/^rgba?\\s*\\(/.test(val) && /,\\s*[\\d.]+\\s*\\)$/.test(val) && !/,\\s*1\\s*\\)$/.test(val)) {\n   202→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Transparence (alpha) non supportée en CMJN\" });\n   203→      }\n   204→      if (/^hsla?\\s*\\(/.test(val)) {\n   205→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Couleur HSL — convertir en hex pour l'impression\" });\n   206→      }\n   207→      if (val === \"#000000\" || val === \"#000\" || val.toLowerCase() === \"black\") {\n   208→        colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Noir pur — utiliser un noir riche (ex: #1C1C1C) pour l'impression\" });\n   209→      }\n   210→      // Detect highly saturated colors likely out of CMYK gamut\n   211→      const hex = parseHex(val);\n   212→      if (hex) {\n   213→        const [r, g, _b] = hex;\n   214→        const max = Math.max(r, g, _b);\n   215→        const min = Math.min(r, g, _b);\n   216→        if (max === 255 && min === 0 && (r === 0 || g === 0 || _b === 0)) {\n   217→          colorWarnings.push({ id: b.id, type: b.type, property: prop, value: val, reason: \"Couleur très saturée — hors gamut CMJN probable\" });\n   218→        }\n   219→      }\n   220→    }\n   221→  }\n   222→\n   223→  return { structuralLayers: [...structuralIds], overlaps, outOfBounds, bleedZone, spacingGroups, colorWarnings };\n   224→}\n   225→\n   226→function parseHex(val: string): [number, number, number] | null {\n   227→  const m3 = val.match(/^#([0-9a-f])([0-9a-f])([0-9a-f])$/i);\n   228→  if (m3) return [parseInt(m3[1] + m3[1], 16), parseInt(m3[2] + m3[2], 16), parseInt(m3[3] + m3[3], 16)];\n   229→  const m6 = 86→  // Clean up document-level listeners\n    87→  if (cleanupListeners) { cleanupListeners(); cleanupListeners = null; }\n    88→  previewImg = null;\n    89→\n    90→  if (apply && currentElId && 158→\n   159→    draft.cropX = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, dragStartCropX + dcx));\n   160→    draft.cropY = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, dragStartCropY + dcy));\n   161→    updatePreview();\n   162→  };\n   163→\n   164→  const onUp = () => { isDragging = false; };\n   165→  document.addEventListener('mousemove', onMove);\n   166→  document.addEventListener('mouseup', onUp);\n   167→  cleanupListeners = If landscape: `w = f.h, h = f.w`. Screen formats always use their definition dimensions unchanged.\n\n### Background Rendering\n\nSVG export: a `<rect>` fills the full `viewBox` with `fill=bg` before any elements. The `viewBox` is `\"0 0 w h\"` (or `\"-bleed -bleed w+2b h+2b\"` with bleed). Width/height attributes are `{w}mm` / `{h}mm`.\n\n---\n\n## BaseElement (all elements inherit)\n\n```\nid: string            — auto-generated \"e{n}\" (e.g. \"e1\", \"e2\")\nname?: string         — optional human label (undefined if not provided)\ntype: string          — discriminant: \"text\" | \"image\" | \"rect\" | \"line\" | \"group\"\nopacity: number       — default 1, range [0, 1]\nrotation: number      — degrees, default 0\n```\n\n---\n\n## TextElement\n\n### All Properties with Defaults (`src/types.ts` line 35, `src/handlers.ts` lines 321-336)\n\n```\ntype: \"text\"\nx: number             — mm from left, required (no default)\ny: number             — mm from top, baseline position (not top of glyph)\ntext: string          — raw content, newlines supported via \"\\n\"\nfontSize: number      — mm, default 8\nfontFamily: string    — default \"Libre Baskerville\"\nfontWeight: string    — default \"bold\"\nfontStyle: string     — default \"normal\"\nfill: string          — CSS color, default \"#1C1C1C\"\ntextAnchor: string    — \"start\" | \"middle\" | \"end\", default \"start\"\nmaxWidth: number|null — mm, default null (no wrapping)\nopacity: number       — inherited from BaseElement, default 1\nrotation: number      — degrees, default 0\nname?: string         — optional\n```\n\n### SVG Rendering (`src/svg.ts` lines 147-155)\n\nGenerates `<text>` with one `<tspan>` per line:\n\n```xml\n<text x=\"{x}\" y=\"{y}\" font-family=\"{fontFamily}\" font-size=\"{fontSize}\"\n      font-weight=\"{fontWeight}\" font-style=\"{fontStyle}\"\n      fill=\"{fill}\" text-anchor=\"{textAnchor}\" [opacity] [transform]>\n  <tspan x=\"{x}\" dy=\"0\">{line1}</tspan>\n  <tspan x=\"{x}\" dy=\"{fontSize * 1.3}\">{line2}</tspan>\n  ...\n</text>\n```\n\nKey details:\n- First tspan: `dy=\"0\"`. Subsequent tspans: `dy=fontSize * 1.3` (the only line-height, hardcoded 130%).\n- All tspans repeat `x=\"{el.x}\"` so they reset to the same horizontal anchor on each line.\n- Text content is XML-escaped: `&amp; &lt; &gt; &quot;`.\n- Rotation pivot: `(x, y)` — i.e., the baseline anchor point itself.\n\n### Client Rendering Difference (`client/render.ts` lines 274-308)\n\nIdentical tspan structure. Additional behaviour: when the element is selected and has `maxWidth`, the client draws a dashed blue `<rect>` guide box showing the wrap boundary (`stroke=\"#3B82F6\"`, `stroke-dasharray=\"1.5,1\"`, `stroke-width=0.3`).\n\n### Text Baseline and BBox (`src/layout.ts` lines 19-30)\n\nThe `y` coordinate is the text baseline. The bbox top is `y - fontSize * 0.85` (approximate cap-height offset). Height = `fontSize * lineCount * 1.3`. Width = measured via opentype.js `getAdvanceWidth` (or fallback `charCount * fontSize * 0.55`).\n\n`textAnchor` shifts the bbox:\n- `\"middle\"` → `bboxX = x - width/2`\n- `\"end\"` → `bboxX = x - width`\n- `\"start\"` → `bboxX = x`\n\n### Wrapping Behavior (`src/fonts.ts` lines 54-74)\n\nWhen `maxWidth !== null`: splits text into paragraphs on `\"\\n\"`, then greedily packs words into lines measuring each candidate with opentype.js `getAdvanceWidth`. If no font is loaded, falls back to `charCount * fontSize * 0.55`.\n\nWhen `maxWidth === null`: simply splits on `\"\\n\"`, no width-based wrapping.\n\n### Font Support (`src/fonts.ts` lines 15-40)\n\nTwo families are loaded from TTF files at server startup:\n\n**Libre Baskerville** (variable weight font `LibreBaskerville[wght].ttf` and `LibreBaskerville-Italic[wght].ttf`):\n- `normal` / `normal` (upright)\n- `bold` / `normal`\n- `normal` / `italic`\n- `bold` / `italic`\n\n**Source Sans 3** (variable weight `SourceSans3[wght].ttf` and `SourceSans3-Italic[wght].ttf`):\n- `normal` / `normal`\n- `\"300\"` / `normal`\n- `\"600\"` / `normal`\n- `bold` / `normal`\n- `\"700\"` / `normal`\n- `normal` / `italic`\n\nFont key format: `\"{family}|{weight}|{style}\"`. Any unrecognised combination falls back to the first loaded font. The `fontFamily` and `fontWeight` strings in SVG attributes are passed verbatim — the browser/renderer uses them directly.\n\n---\n\n## ImageElement\n\n### All Properties with Defaults (`src/types.ts` lines 49-81, `src/handlers.ts` lines 363-393)\n\n```\ntype: \"image\"\nx: number             — mm from left\ny: number             — mm from top\nwidth: number         — frame width mm (required, no default)\nheight: number        — frame height mm (required, no default)\npath: string          — relative asset path (e.g. \"photo.jpg\")\nhref: string|null     — base64 data URI (loaded at add time, excluded from JSON display)\npreserveAspectRatio: string — legacy field, default \"xMidYMid slice\"\n                             (used only in fill mode without flipTransform)\nnaturalWidth: number  — source pixel width (read from file metadata)\nnaturalHeight: number — source pixel height\n\n-- Crop & Fit --\nobjectFit: \"cover\"|\"contain\"|\"fill\"  — default \"cover\"\ncropX: number         — 0–1, horizontal pan, default 0.5 (centered)\ncropY: number         — 0–1, vertical pan, default 0.5 (centered)\ncropZoom: number      — 1 = tight cover, >1 zooms in, default 1\n\n-- Flip --\nflipH: boolean        — horizontal mirror, default false\nflipV: boolean        — vertical mirror, default false\n\n-- Filters --\nbrightness: number    — 50–150 (UI range), 100 = neutral, default 100\ncontrast: number      — 50–150 (UI range), 100 = neutral, default 100\ngrayscale: number     — 0–100, 0 = color, 100 = B&W, default 0\n\n-- Border --\nborderWidth: number   — mm stroke, default 0\nborderColor: string   — CSS color, default \"#000000\"\nborderRadius: number  — mm corner radius, default 0\n\n-- Shadow --\nshadowX: number       — mm horizontal offset, default 0\nshadowY: number       — mm vertical offset, default 0\nshadowBlur: number    — mm blur radius, default 0\nshadowColor: string   — CSS color, default \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\"\n\nopacity: number       — default 1\nrotation: number      — degrees, default 0\nname?: string\n```\n\n### Object Fit Modes\n\n**cover** (`src/svg.ts` lines 102-117): Image is scaled so its smaller dimension fills the frame. Formula:\n```\nbaseScale = max(frameW/natW, frameH/natH)\nscale = baseScale * cropZoom\nimgW = natW * scale\nimgH = natH * scale\nimgX = el.x - (imgW - frameW) * cropX\nimgY = el.y - (imgH - frameH) * cropY\n```\nA `<clipPath>` is pushed to `<defs>` as `<clipPath id=\"c_{id}\"><rect x y w h/></clipPath>` and applied via `clip-path=\"url(#c_{id})\"`.\n\n**contain** (`src/svg.ts` lines 119-126): Image placed with `preserveAspectRatio=\"xMidYMid meet\"`. No clip path. Letterboxed inside the frame.\n\n**fill** (`src/svg.ts` lines 128-137): Image stretched with `preserveAspectRatio=\"none\"` (or the legacy `preserveAspectRatio` field value if no flip).\n\n### Flip Transform Pattern (`src/svg.ts` lines 92-98)\n\nApplied as a CSS/SVG transform around the frame center:\n```\ntranslate(cx, cy) scale(flipH, flipV) translate(-cx, -cy)\n```\nwhere `cx = el.x + el.width/2`, `cy = el.y + el.height/2`, `flipH = -1 or 1`, `flipV = -1 or 1`.\n\nIn cover mode, the flip is on the inner `<g>` containing the image (so it flips within the clip). In contain/fill mode, it merges with the outer rotation group's transform.\n\n### SVG Filter Chain (`src/svg.ts` lines 36-56)\n\nFilter is generated in `<defs>` as `<filter id=\"f_{id}\">` and applied via `filter=\"url(#f_{id})\"` on the `<image>` element.\n\nCondition: filter is built if any of `brightness !== 100`, `contrast !== 100`, `grayscale > 0`, `shadowBlur > 0`, `shadowX !== 0`, `shadowY !== 0`.\n\nPipeline order:\n1. **Shadow** (if present): `<feDropShadow dx=shadowX dy=shadowY stdDeviation=shadowBlur flood-color=shadowColor flood-opacity=\"1\" result=\"shadow\"/>`\n2. **Grayscale**: `<feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\" values=\"{1 - grayscale/100}\" in=\"{shadow|SourceGraphic}\" result=\"gray\"/>`\n3. **Brightness + Contrast**: `<feComponentTransfer in=\"gray\">` with three `<feFuncR|G|B type=\"linear\" slope=\"{b*c}\" intercept=\"{(1-c)*0.5}\"/>` where `b = brightness/100`, `c = contrast/100`.\n\nThe client (`client/render.ts` lines 116-141) generates an identical filter but additionally sets `x=\"-20%\"` `y=\"-20%\"` `width=\"140%\"` `height=\"140%\"` on the `<filter>` element to prevent clipping the shadow.\n\n### Clip Path — Border Radius Support\n\nIn the server SVG (`src/svg.ts` line 114), the cover-mode `<clipPath>` always uses a plain `<rect>` (no `rx`). Border radius does NOT round the image clip in the SVG export.\n\nIn the client (`client/render.ts` lines 147-155), the cover-mode `<clipPath>` uses `<rect rx=el.borderRadius>` when `el.borderRadius > 0` — so rounded image corners work in the live preview but NOT in the exported SVG.\n\n### Border Rendering (`src/svg.ts` lines 140-142, `client/render.ts` lines 261-270)\n\nA separate `<rect>` with `fill=\"none\"` is appended after the image group:\n```xml\n<rect x y width height fill=\"none\" stroke=borderColor stroke-width=borderWidth rx=borderRadius/>\n```\n\n### Full SVG Output Structure for Image\n\n```xml\n<g [opacity] [transform=rotate]>\n  <g clip-path=\"url(#c_{id})\" [transform=flip]>   <!-- cover mode -->\n    <image x imgX y imgY width imgW height imgH href=... preserveAspectRatio=\"none\" [filter]/>\n  </g>\n  <rect x y w h fill=\"transparent\"/>   <!-- hit area, client only -->\n  <rect x y w h fill=\"none\" stroke=borderColor stroke-width=borderWidth rx=borderRadius/>  <!-- border -->\n</g>\n```\n\n---\n\n## RectElement\n\n### All Properties with Defaults (`src/types.ts` lines 83-93, `src/handlers.ts` lines 415-428)\n\n```\ntype: \"rect\"\nx: number         — mm from left\ny: number         — mm from top\nwidth: number     — mm (required)\nheight: number    — mm (required)\nfill: string      — CSS color, default \"#000000\"\nstroke: string    — CSS color or \"none\", default \"none\"\nstrokeWidth: number — mm, default 0\nrx: number        — corner radius mm, default 0\nopacity: number   — default 1\nrotation: number  — degrees, default 0\nname?: string\n```\n\n### SVG Rendering (`src/svg.ts` line 78)\n\nSingle self-closing element:\n```xml\n<rect x=\"{x}\" y=\"{y}\" width=\"{w}\" height=\"{h}\"\n      fill=\"{fill}\" stroke=\"{stroke}\" stroke-width=\"{strokeWidth}\" rx=\"{rx}\"\n      [opacity] [transform]/>\n```\n\n### BBox (`src/layout.ts` line 12)\n\n`{ x: el.x, y: el.y, w: el.width, h: el.height }` — ignores stroke width, rotation ignored.\n\n---\n\n## LineElement\n\n### All Properties with Defaults (`src/types.ts` lines 95-103, `src/handlers.ts` lines 451-459)\n\n```\ntype: \"line\"\nx1: number        — start x mm\ny1: number        — start y mm\nx2: number        — end x mm\ny2: number        — end y mm\nstroke: string    — CSS color, default \"#000000\"\nstrokeWidth: number — mm, default 0.5\nopacity: number   — default 1\nrotation: number  — degrees, default 0\nname?: string\n```\n\nNo `fill`, no `rx`, no shadow, no filters.\n\n### SVG Rendering (`src/svg.ts` line 81)\n\n```xml\n<line x1=\"{x1}\" y1=\"{y1}\" x2=\"{x2}\" y2=\"{y2}\"\n      stroke=\"{stroke}\" stroke-width=\"{strokeWidth}\"\n      [opacity] [transform]/>\n```\n\n### BBox (`src/layout.ts` lines 14-17)\n\n```\nx = min(x1, x2)\ny = min(y1, y2)\nw = |x2 - x1| or 0.5 (minimum to avoid zero-size box)\nh = |y2 - y1| or 0.5\n```\n\n### Rotation Pivot (`src/svg.ts` lines 64-66)\n\nFor lines, the rotation center is `((x1+x2)/2, (y1+y2)/2)` — the midpoint of the line.\n\n---\n\n## GroupElement\n\n### All Properties (`src/types.ts` lines 105-108)\n\n```\ntype: \"group\"\nid: string\nname?: string\nchildren: Element[]   — arbitrary depth, any element types including nested groups\nopacity: number       — default 1 (at creation: handlers.ts line 822)\nrotation: number      — default 0 (at creation: handlers.ts line 823)\n```\n\nGroups have no own geometry. No `x`, `y`, `width`, `height`, `fill`, `stroke`.\n\n### SVG Rendering (`src/svg.ts` lines 16-28)\n\n```xml\n<g id=\"{id}\" [opacity] [transform=rotate(rot, cx, cy)]>\n  <!-- children rendered recursively -->\n</g>\n```\n\nThe rotation pivot `(cx, cy)` is computed from the group's `bbox()` center: `cx = bbox.x + bbox.w/2`, `cy = bbox.y + bbox.h/2`.\n\n### BBox Computation (`src/layout.ts` lines 32-43)\n\nUnion of all children's bboxes: min of all `child.bbox.x`, min of all `child.bbox.y`, max of `child.bbox.x + child.bbox.w`, max of `child.bbox.y + child.bbox.h`. Empty group returns `{0,0,0,0}`.\n\nRotation is NOT factored into the bbox — the bbox is axis-aligned from the pre-rotation coordinates.\n\n### Client Rendering Difference (`client/render.ts` lines 98-105)\n\nClient uses `<g data-group=\"{id}\">` attribute (not `id=`). Opacity applied the same way. Rotation is NOT applied to the group wrapper in the client — groups only propagate opacity. Children are rendered recursively inside the group `<g>`.\n\n### Constraints\n\n- All elements to be grouped must be siblings (same parent array).\n- Cycles prevented: cannot add an element into one of its own descendants.\n- Ungrouping flattens children into the parent array at the group's position.\n\n---\n\n## Transform Patterns Summary\n\nAll transforms use SVG `transform=\"rotate(degrees, cx, cy)\"`:\n\n| Element type | Pivot point |\n|---|---|\n| rect | `(x + width/2, y + height/2)` |\n| image | `(x + width/2, y + height/2)` |\n| text | `(x, y)` — the baseline anchor |\n| line | `((x1+x2)/2, (y1+y2)/2)` — midpoint |\n| group | `(bbox.x + bbox.w/2, bbox.y + bbox.h/2)` — bbox center |\n\nFlip uses a separate `translate-scale-translate` pattern (not `rotate`).\n\n---\n\n## SVG Filter Primitives Used\n\nOnly images use filters. The filter chain (when any condition is met):\n\n| Primitive | Condition | Key attributes |\n|---|---|---|\n| `<feDropShadow>` | `shadowBlur > 0 OR shadowX != 0 OR shadowY != 0` | `dx`, `dy`, `stdDeviation`, `flood-color`, `flood-opacity=\"1\"` |\n| `<feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\">` | `grayscale > 0` | `values = 1 - grayscale/100` |\n| `<feComponentTransfer>` + 3x `<feFuncR|G|B>` | `brightness != 100 OR contrast != 100` | `type=\"linear\"`, `slope = b*c`, `intercept = (1-c)*0.5` |\n\nShadow result name: `\"shadow\"`. Color/contrast input comes from either `SourceGraphic` (no shadow) or `\"shadow\"`. Color matrix result: `\"gray\"`. Component transfer reads from `\"gray\"`.\n\n---\n\n## Clip Path Patterns\n\n| Use case | Structure |\n|---|---|\n| Image cover crop (server SVG) | `<clipPath id=\"c_{id}\"><rect x y w h/></clipPath>` (no rx) |\n| Image cover crop (client, borderRadius=0) | `<clipPath id=\"c_{id}\"><rect x y w h/></clipPath>` |\n| Image cover crop (client, borderRadius>0) | `<clipPath id=\"c_{id}\"><rect x y w h rx=borderRadius/></clipPath>` |\n\nThe maxWidth text guide in the client is rendered as a dashed `<rect>` — not a clip path.\n\n---\n\n## CSS vs SVG: Client vs Export Differences\n\n| Feature | SVG Export (server) | Client (D3) |\n|---|---|---|\n| Border radius on image clip | Not applied (plain rect in clipPath) | Applied if `borderRadius > 0` |\n| Filter `<filter>` region | No explicit x/y/w/h (browser default 10% overflow) | Explicit `-20% -20% 140% 140%` to contain shadow |\n| Image hit area | Not present | Transparent `<rect>` appended for drag events |\n| Group rotation | Applied as `transform` on `<g>` | NOT applied to group `<g>` (client omits group rotation) |\n| Image filters preview | SVG filter | CSS `filter: brightness() contrast() grayscale()` on `<img>` in the editor modal |\n| Flip preview in editor | Not applicable | CSS `transform: scale(sx, sy)` on `<img>` |\n| Inspector overlay | Not present | Dashed bounding boxes + pill labels with `Outfit, sans-serif` |\n| Snap guides | Not present | `#3B82F6` dashed lines, `stroke-dasharray=\"2,2\"`, `stroke-width=0.5` |\n| Bleed overlay | Not present | Four red `rgba(255,0,0,0.08)` rects + dashed border `3mm` from edges |\n| Selection rect | Not present | `<rect class=\"selection-rect\">` 1mm padding around element bbox |\n\n---\n\n## Image Editor Modal Controls\n\nThe modal (`client/image-editor.ts`) provides interactive editing of:\n\n| Control | Type | Range | Default |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| objectFit | 3-button toggle | cover / contain / fill | cover |\n| cropZoom (wheel) | scroll | 1–5, step 0.05 | 1 |\n| cropZoom (slider id=\"ieZoom\") | range | 1–5, step 0.1 | 1 |\n| cropX / cropY | mouse drag on preview | 0–1 | 0.5 |\n| flipH | toggle button | true/false | false |\n| flipV | toggle button | true/false | false |\n| brightness (id=\"ieBrightness\") | range | 50–150, step 1 | 100 |\n| contrast (id=\"ieContrast\") | range | 50–150, step 1 | 100 |\n| grayscale (id=\"ieGrayscale\") | range | 0–100, step 1 | 0 |\n\nPreview uses CSS `filter: brightness(x%) contrast(x%) grayscale(x%)` for live preview. Crop pan converts pixel drag delta into cropX/cropY delta by computing the excess image size beyond the frame and dividing.\n\nChanges are committed via `sendUpdate` (WebSocket to server) only when \"Apply\" is clicked. Cancel discards. Undo/redo entry is pushed on apply.\n\n---\n\n## Coordinate System\n\nAll coordinates (`x`, `y`, `x1`, `y1`, `x2`, `y2`, `width`, `height`, `fontSize`, `strokeWidth`, `borderWidth`, `shadowX`, `shadowY`, `shadowBlur`, `borderRadius`, `rx`, `cropZoom`, `maxWidth`) are in **millimetres**. The SVG `viewBox` uses these mm values directly. The `width` and `height` SVG root attributes are suffixed with `mm` (e.g. `width=\"297mm\"`). Screen pixels in the client UI are mapped via a zoom/pan transform managed in `client/zoom.ts`."}],"stop_reason":"end_turn","stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":5924,"cache_read_input_tokens":62215,"output_tokens":6358,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":5924},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"}},"requestId":"req_011CZ1rnTSz2WNkW2Yxx5JvT","type":"assistant","uuid":"7ded0ee8-835f-4791-a16b-0439966d6764","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:23:26.732Z","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}
